prajanayanty eṣu lokeṣu pratitiṣṭhantiPB  sa etaṃ tryahaṃ punaḥ prāyauṅkta tena ṣaḍahena ṣaṭkratūn prājanayatPB  yad eṣa ṣaḍaho bhavati ṛtūn eva prajanayanti ṛtuṣu pratitiṣṭhantiPB  sa etaṃ ṣaḍahaṃ punaḥ prāyuṅkta tābhyāṃ dvābhyāṃ ṣaḍahābhyāṃ dvādaśamasaḥ prājanayatPB  yad etau ṣaḍahau bhavato māsān eva prajanayanti māseṣu pratitiṣṭhantiPB  sa etau dvau ṣaḍahau punaḥ prayuṅkta taiś caturbhiḥ ṣaḍahaiś caturviṃśatim ardhamāsān prājanayatPB  yad ete catvāraḥ ṣaḍahā bhavanty ardhamāsān eva prajanayanty ardhamāseṣu pratitiṣṭhantiPB  sa idaṃ bhuvanaṃ prajanayitva pṛṣṭhyena ṣaḍahena vīryam ātmany adhattaPB  yad eṣaḥ pṛṣṭhyaḥ ṣaḍaho bhavati vīrya evāntataḥ pratitiṣṭhantiPB  tena māsān saṃvvatsaraṃ prājanayad yad eṣa māso bhavati saṃvvatsaram eva prajanayanti saṃvvatsare pratitiṣṭhantiPB  prāyaṇīyam etad ahar bhavatiPB  prāyaṇīyena vā ahnā devāḥ svargaṃ lokaṃ prāyan yat prāyaṃs tat prāyaṇīyasya prāyaṇīyatvamPB  tasmāt prāyaṇīyasyāhna ṛtvijā bhavitavyam etad dhi svargasya lokasya nediṣṭhaṃ ya etasyartviṅ na bhavati hīyate svargāl lokātPB  caturviṃśaṃ bhavatiPB  caturviṃśatyakṣarā gāyatrī tejo brahmavarcasaṃ gāyatrī teja eva brahmavarcasam ārabhya prayantiPB  caturviṃśaṃ bhavati caturviṃśo vai saṃvvatsaraḥ sākṣād eva saṃvvatsaram ārabhantePB  yāvatyaś caturviṃśasyokthasya stotrīyās tāvatyaḥ saṃvvatsarasya rātrayaḥ stotrīyābhir eva tat saṃvvatsaram āpnuvantiPB  pañcadaśastotrāṇi bhavanti pañcadaśārdhamāsasya rātrayo rdhamāsaśa eva tat saṃvvatsaram āpnuvantiPB  pañcadaśa stotrāṇi pañcadaśaśastrāṇi samāso māsaśa eva tat saṃvvatsaram āpnuvantiPB  tad āhur īrma iva vā eṣā hotrā yad acchāvākyā yad acchāvākam anusaṃtiṣṭhataīśvarermā bhavitor iti yady ukthaṃ smātraikakubhañcodvaṃśīyañcāntataḥ pratiṣṭhāpyevīryaṃ vā ete samanī vīrya evāntataḥ pratitiṣṭhantiPB  atho khalv āhur agniṣṭomam eva kāryam eṣa vai yajñaḥ svargyo yad agniṣṭoma ūrdhvo hi hotāram anusaṃtiṣṭhatePB  dvādaśastotrāṇy agniṣṭomo dvādaśa māsāḥ saṃvvatsaras tena saṃvvatsarasaṃmitodvādaśa stotraṇi dvādaśa śastrāṇi tac caturviṃśatiś caturviṃśatir ardhamāsāḥ saṃvvatsarastena saṃvvatsarasaṃmitaḥPB  atho khalv āhur uktham eva kāryam ahnaḥ samṛddhyaiPB  sarvāṇi rūpāṇi kriyante sarvaṃ hy etāhnāpyatePB  pavante vājasātaye somāḥ sahasrapājasa iti sahasravatī pratipat kāryāPB  saṃvvatsarasya rūpaṃ sarvan evainān etayā punāti sarvān abhivadati PB  atho khalv āhuḥ pavasva vāco agriya ity eva kāryā mukhaṃ vā etat saṃvvatsarasya yad vāco graṃ mukhata eva tat saṃvvatsaram ārabhante  PB  mithunam iva vā eṣā vyāhṛtiḥ pavasveti puṃso rūpaṃ vāca iti striyāḥ someti puṃso rūpaṃ citrābhir iti striyā mithunam evaibhyo yajñamukhe  dadhāti prajananāya  PB  agne yuṅkṣvā hi ye taveti jarābodhīyam agniṣṭoma sāma kāryaṃ yuktenaiva saṃvvatsareṇa prayanti caturviṃśatyakṣarāsu bhavati caturviṃśasya PB  atho khalv āhur yajñāyajñīyam eva kāryamPB  panthā vai yajñāyajñīyaṃ patha eva tan na yantiPB  abhīvarto brahmasāma bhavatiPB  abhīvartena vai devāḥ svargaṃ lokam abhyavartanta yad abhīvarto brahmasāma bhavati svargasya lokasyābhivṛttyaiPB  ekākṣaraṇidhano bhavaty ekākṣarā vai vāg vācaiva tad ārabhya svargaṃ lokaṃ yantiPB  sāmneto yanty ṛcā punar āyantiPB  sāma vai asau loka ṛg ayaṃ yad itaḥ sāmnā yanti svargaṃ lokam ārabhya yanti yad ṛcā punar āyanty asmin loke pratitiṣṭhantiPB  yat sāmāvasṛjeyur ava svargāl lokāt padyeran yad ṛcam anusṛjeyur naśyeyur asmāl lokātPB  samānaṃ sāma bhavaty anyonyaḥ pragātho nyadanyad dhi citram adhvānam avagacchann etiPB  vṛṣā vā eṣa retodhā yad abhīvartaḥ pragātheṣu reto dadhad eti yad itaḥsamānaṃ sāma bhavaty anyonyaḥ pragātho reta eva tad dadhati yat parastāt samānaḥpragātho bhavaty anyadanyat sāma reta eva tad dhitaṃ prajanayantiPB  sāmnetaḥ pragāthāṃ dugdhe pragāthena parastāt sāmāni dugdhe salomatvāyaPB  yo vā adhvānaṃ punar nivartayanti nainaṃ te gacchanti ye punar nivartaṃ yanti te gacchatiPB  ya āstutaṃ kurvate yathā dugdhām upasīded evaṃ tatPB  ye nāstutaṃ yaṃ kāmaṃ kāmayante tam abhyaśnuvate PB  brahmavādino vadanti yātayāmāḥ saṃvvatsarā ayātayāmā iti te nāyātayāmeti vaktavyaṃ punar anyāni stotrāṇi nivartanta ūrdhvam eva PB  pañcasu māḥsu bārhatāḥ pragāthā āpyantePB  teṣv āpteṣu chandasī saṃyujyaitavyamPB  tisra uṣṇihaḥ syur ekā gāyatrī tās tisro bṛhatyo bhavantiPB  tad āhuḥ saṃśara iva vā eṣa cchandasāṃ yad dve chandasī saṃyuñjantītiPB  catur uttarair eva cchandobhir etavyamPB  paśavo vai caturuttarāṇi cchandasāṃsi paśubhir eva tat svargaṃ lokam ākramam ānayantiPB  ekaṃ gāyatrīm ekāham upeyur ekāmuṣṇiham ekāham ekām anuṣṭubham ekāhaṃbṛhatyā pañcamāsa iyuḥ paṅktim ekāham upeyus triṣṭubhā ṣaṣṭhaṃ māsam īyuḥ śvo viṣuvānbhaviteti jagatīm upeyuḥPB  tad āhur anavakḷptāni vā etāni cchandāṃsi madhyandine bṛhatyā caiva triṣṭubhā caitavyamPB  ete vai chandasī vīryavatī ete pratyakṣaṃ madhyandinasya rūpamPB  rathantare hani bṛhatī kāryaitad vai rathantarasya svam āyatanaṃ yadbṛhatī sva eva tad āyatane rathantaraṃ pratitiṣṭhati bārhate hani triṣṭup kāryaitadvai bṛhataḥ svam āyatanaṃ yat triṣṭup sva eva tad āyatane bṛhadrathantare pratitiṣṭhantī itaḥPB  trayastriṃśatā pragāthair etavyaṃ trayastriṃśad devatā devatāsv eva pratitiṣṭhantoyanti caturviṃśatyaitavyaṃ caturviṃśatir ardhamāsāḥ saṃvvatsaraḥ saṃvvatsara evapratitiṣṭhanto yanti dvādaśabhir etavyaṃ dvādaśa māsāḥ saṃvvatsaraḥ saṃvvatsara evapratitiṣṭhanto yanti ṣaḍbhir etavyaṃ ṣaḍ ṛtava ṛtuṣv eva pratitiṣṭhanto yanti caturbhiretavyaṃ catuṣpādāḥ paśavaḥ paśuṣv eva pratitiṣṭhanto yanti tribhir etavyaṃ trayaime lokā eṣv eva lokeṣu pratitiṣṭhanto yanti dvābhyām etavyaṃ dvipād yajamānaḥ svargasyalokasyākrāntyā anyenānyena hi padā puruṣaḥ pratitiṣṭhann etiPB  svarasāmāna ete bhavantePB  svarbhānur vā āsur ādityaṃ tamasāvidhyat taṃ devāḥ svarair aspṛṇvan yat svarasāmāno bhavanty ādityasya spṛtyaiPB  parair vai devā ādityaṃ svargaṃ lokam apārayan yad aparayaṃs tat parāṇāṃ paratvaṃPB  pārayanty enaṃ parāṇi ya evaṃv vedaPB  saptadaśā bhavantiPB  prajāpatir vai saptadaśaḥ prajāpatim evopayantiPB  anuṣṭup chandaso bhavanty ānuṣṭubho vai prajāpatiḥ sākṣād eva prajāpatim ārabhantePB  trayaḥ purastāt trayaḥ parastād bhavantiPB  devā vā ādityasya svargāl lokād avapādād abibhayus tam etaiḥ stomaiḥ saptadaśair adṛṃhan yad ete stomābhavanty ādityasya dhṛtyaiPB  catustriṃśā bhavanti varṣma vai catustriṃśo varṣmaṇaivainaṃ saṃmimate PB  tasya parācīnātipādād abibhayus taṃ sarvaiḥ stomaiḥ paryārṣan viśvajidabhijidbhyāṃ vīryaṃ vā etau stomau vīryeṇaiva tad ādityaṃ  paryuṣanti dhṛtyai PB  anavapādāyānatipādāyaPB  tad āhuḥ kartapraskanda iva vā eṣa yat trayastriṃśataḥ saptadaśam upayantīti pṛṣṭhyo ntaraḥ kāryaḥPB  tasya yat saptadaśam ahas tad uttamaṃ kāryaṃ salomatvāyaPB  tad āhur udaraṃ vā eṣa stomānāṃ yat saptadaśo yat saptadaśaṃ madhyato nirhareyur aśanāyavaḥ prajāḥ syur aśanāyavaḥ sattriṇaḥPB  trayastriṃśād eva saptadaśa upetyo varṣma vai trayastriṃśo varṣma saptadaśo varṣmaṇa eva tad varṣmābhisaṃkrāmantiPB  nānāhur ukthāḥ kāryā iti yady ukthāḥ syuḥPB  paśavo vā ukthāni śāntiḥ paśavaḥ śāntenaiva tad viṣuvantam upayantiPB  tad āhur vivīvadham iva vā etad yad agniṣṭomo viṣuvān agniṣṭomau viśvajidabhijitāv athetara ukthāḥ syur itiPB  agniṣṭomā eva sarve kāryāḥPB  vīryaṃ vā agniṣṭomo vīrya eva madhyataḥ pratitiṣṭhanti nava saṃstutā bhavanti nava prāṇāḥ praṇeṣv eva pratitiṣṭhantiPB  viṣuvān eṣa bhavatiPB  devaloko vā eṣa yad viṣuvān devaokam eva tad abhyārohantiPB  ekaviṃśo bhavaty ekaviṃśo vā asya bhuvanasyāditya ādityalokam eva tad abhyārohantiPB  dvādaśa māsāḥ pañcartavas traya ime lokā asāv āditya ekaviṃśaḥPB  madhyata eva yajñasya pratitiṣṭhantiPB  vāyo śukro ayāmi ta iti śukravatī pratipad bhavaty ādityasya rūpamPB  vāyur vā etaṃ devatānām ānaśe nuṣṭup chandasaṃ yad ato nyā pratipat syāt pradahetPB  yanti vā ete prāṇādityāhur ye gāyatryāḥ pratipado yantīti yad vayavyā bhavanti tena prāṇān na yanti prāṇo hi vāyuḥPB  atho śamayanty evainam etayā śantir hi vāyuḥPB  ā yāhi somapītaya iti saumī pāvamānīPB  niyutvatī bhavati paśavo vai niyutaḥ śāntiḥ paśavaḥ śāntenaiva tad ādityam upayantiPB  divākīrtyasāmā bhavatiPB  svarbhānur vā āsur ādityaṃ tamasāvidhyat tasya devā divākīrtyais tamopāghnan yad divākīrtyāni bhavanti tama evāsmād apaghnanti raśmayo vā eta ādityasyayad divākīrtyāni raśmibhir eva tad ādityaṃ sākṣād ārabhantePB  bhrājābhrāje pavamānamukhe bhavato mukhata evāsya tābhyāṃ tamo paghnanti PB  mahādivākīrtyaṃ ca vikarṇaṃ ca madhyato bhavato madhyata evāsya tābhyāṃ tamo paghnanti bhāsam antato bhavati patta evāsya tena  tamo paghnanti PB  daśastobhaṃ bhavti daśākṣarā virāḍ virājy eva pratitiṣṭhantiPB  yat tv ity āhuḥ ṣaḍbhir ito māsair adhvānaṃ yanti ṣaḍbhiḥ punar āyanti kva tarhi svargo loko yasya kāmāya sattram āsata itiPB  mūrdhānaṃ diva iti svargaṃ lokam ārabhantePB  aratiṃ pṛthivyā ity asmiṃ loke pratitiṣṭhantiPB  vaiśvānaram ṛta ājātam agnim iti viṣuvata eva tad rūpaṃ kriyatePB  kaviṃ samrājam atitihiṃ janānām ity annādyam evopayantiPB  āsan nāpātraṃ janayanta devā iti jāyanta evaPB  tat triṣṭub jagatīṣu bhavati traiṣṭubhjāgato vā ādityo yad ato nyāsu syād ava svargāl lokāt padyeranPB  samrāḍvatīṣu bhavati sāmrājyaṃ vai svargo lokaḥ svarga eva loke pratitiṣṭhantiPB  ātmā vā eṣa saṃvvatsarasya yad viṣuvān pakṣāv etāv abhito bhavato yenaceto bhīvartena yanti yaś ca parasmāt pragātho bhavati tāv ubhau viṣuvati kāryaupakṣāv eva tad yajñasyātman pratidadhati svargasya lokasya samaṣṭyaiPB  indra kratuṃ na ābhareti pragātho bhavatiPB  vasiṣṭho vā etaṃ putrahato paśyat sa prajayā paśubhiḥ prājāyata yad eṣa pragātho bhavati prajātyaiPB  jīvā jyotir aśīmahīti ye vai svasti saṃvvatsaraṃ saṃtaranti te jīvā jyotir aśnuvatePB  māno ajñātā vṛjanā durādhyo māśivāso vakramur iti ye vai stenā ripavas te durādhyas tān eva tad atikrāmatiPB  tvayā vyayaṃ pravataḥ śaśvatīr apo ti śūra tarāma so tisaṃvvatsaro vai pravataḥ śaśvatīr apas tam eva tat taranti PB  adyādyāśvaḥ śvas tvām idā hyo naro vayam enam idā hya iti saṃtanayaḥ pragāthā bhavanti teṣām ekaḥ kāryaḥ salomatvāya śvastanam evābhisaṃtanvanti PB  atho khalv āhur indra kratuṃ na ābharety eva kāryaṃ samṛddhyaiPB  pratyavarohiṇo māsā bhavantiPB  yathā vā ito vṛkṣaṃ rohanty evam enaṃ pratyavarohanti svargam eva virāḍ annādya eva pratitiṣṭhantiPB  dvādaśāhasya daśāhāni bhavantiPB  virāḍ vā eṣā samṛddhā yad daśāhāni virājy eva samṛddhāyāṃ pratitiṣṭhantiPB  pṛṣthāni bhavanti vīryaṃ vai pṛṣṭhāni vīrya eva pratitiṣṭhanti cchandomābhavanti paśavo vai cchandomāḥ paśuṣv eva pratitiṣṭhanty athaitad daśamam ahar āptastomamāptacchanda āptavibhaktikam aniruktaṃ prājāpatyamPB  yad adhyāhur ati tad recayanti tasmān na vyucyamPB  parokṣam anuṣṭubham upayanti prajāpatir vā anuṣṭub yat pratyakṣam upeyuḥ prajāpatim ṛccheyuḥ PB  yo vai sattrasya sad veda sad bhavati vāmadevyaṃ vai sāmnāṃ sad agnir devatānāṃ virāṭ chandasāṃ trayastriṃśaḥ stomānāṃ tāny eva  tad ekadhā saṃbhṛtyottiṣṭhanti PB  brahmavādino vadanti yataḥ sattrād udasthātāsthitād itiPB  ye rathantareṇa stutvottiṣṭhanti te yata uttiṣṭhanti tān brūyād apratiṣṭhānābhaviṣyantīti ye bṛhatā stutyottiṣṭhanti te sthitād uttiṣṭhanti tān brūyāt sthāyukaiṣāṃśrīr bhaviṣyati na vasīyāṃso bhaviṣyantītiPB  ye vāmadevyena stutvottiṣṭhanti te sataḥ sad abhyuttiṣṭhanti pūrṇāt pūrṇam āyatanād āyatanam antarikṣāyatanā hi prajāPB  trayastriṃśadakṣarāsu bhavati trayastriṃśaddevatāsv eva pratiṣṭhāyottiṣṭhantiPB  prājāpatyaṃ vai vāmadevyaṃ prajāpatāv eva pratiṣṭhāyottiṣṭhanti paśavo vai vāmadevyaṃ paśuṣv eva pratiṣṭhāyottiṣṭhantiPB  patnīḥ saṃyājya prāñca udetyāyaṃ sahasramānava ity aticchandasāhavanīyam upatiṣṭhantePB  ime vai lokā aticchandā eṣv eva lokeṣu pratitiṣṭhantiPB  gor iti nidhanaṃ bhavati virājo vā etad rūpaṃ yad gaur virājy eva pratitiṣṭhantiPB  pratyañcaḥ prapadya sārparājñyā ṛgbhiḥ stuvantiPB  arbudaḥ sarpa etābhir mṛtāṃ tvacam apāhata mṛtām evaitābhirs tvacam apaghnatePB  iyaṃ vai sārparājñy asyām eva pratitiṣṭhantiPB  tisṛbhiḥ stuvanti traya ime lokā eṣv eva pratitiṣṭhantiPB  manasopāvartayatiPB  manasā hiṅ karoti manasā prastauti manasodgāyati manasā pratiharati manasā nidhanam upayanty asamāptasya samāptyaiPB  yad vai vācā na samāpnuvanti manasā tat samāpnuvantiPB  pariśrite stuvanti brahmaṇaḥ parigṛhītyaiPB  brahmodyaṃ vadanti brahmavarcasa eva pratitiṣṭhantiPB  caturhotāraṃ hotā vyācaṣṭe stutam eva tad anuśaṃsati nahi tat stutaṃ yad ananuśastamPB  prajāpatiṃ parivadanty āptvevainaṃ tad vyācakṣate tāvad āpāmainam itiPB  gṛhapatir audumbarīṃ dhārayati gṛhapatir vā ūrjo yantorjam evaibhyo yacchatiPB  vācaṃ yacchantiPB  dugdhānīva vai tarhi chandasāṃsi yātayāmāny antargatāni tāny eva tad rasenāpyāyayantiPB  atho śvastanam evābhisaṃtanvantiPB  ātmadakṣiṇaṃ vā etad yat sattramPB  yadā vai puruṣa ātmano vadyati yaṃ kāmaṃ kāmayate tam abhyaśnutePB  dvābhyāṃ lomāvadyati dvābhyāṃ tvacaṃ dvābhyāṃ māṃsaṃ dvābhyām asthi dvābhyāṃ majjānaṃ dvābhyāṃ pīvaś ca lohitaṃ caPB  śikhā anupravapante pāpmānam eva tad apaghnate laghīyāṃsaḥ svargaṃ lokam ayāmetiPB  atho gavām evānurūpā bhavanti sarvasyānnādyasyāvaruddhyaiPB  prajāpatiḥ prajā asṛjata so ricyata so padyata taṃ devā abhisamagacchantate bruvan mahad asmai vrataṃ saṃbharāma yad imaṃ dhinavad iti tasmai yat saṃvvatsaramannaṃ pacyate tat samabharaṃs tad asmai prāyacchaṃs tad avrajayat tad enam adhinonmahan maryā vrataṃ yad imam adhinvīd iti tan mahāvratasya mahāvratatvamPB  prajāpatir vāva mahāṃs tasyaitad vratam annam evaPB  tad āhur madhyaḥ saṃvvatsarasyopetyaṃ madhyato vā annaṃ jagdhaṃ dhinoti PB  tad v āhur yan madhyata upayanty ardham annādyasyāpnuvanty ardhaṃ sambaṭ kurvantīty upariṣṭād eva saṃvvatsarasyopetyaṃ saṃvvatsare  vā annaṃ sarvaṃ pacyate PB  caturviṃśaṃ bhavati caturviṃśo vai saṃvvatsaro nnaṃ pañcaviṃśamPB  yad vā adaś caturviṃśaṃprāyaṇīyaṃ tad etad udayanīyamPB  yat saṃvvatsaram annaṃ saṃbharanti saiṣā pañcaviṃśy upajāyatePB  vāmadevyaṃ mahāvrataṃ kāryamPB  trivṛc chiro bhavatiPB  trivṛd dhy eva śiro loma tvag asthiPB  pāṅkta itara ātmā loma tvaṅ māṃsam asthi majjāPB  sakṛd dhiṅkṛtena śirasā pārācā stuvatePB  tasmāc chiro ṅgāni medyanti nānumedyati na kṛśyanty anukṛśyatiPB  punar abhyāvartam itareṇātmanā stuvate tasmād itara ātmā medyati ca kṛśyati caPB kṛṣṭapacyāś ca kṛṣṭapacyāś caPB  pavasva vāco agriya iti pratipadaṃ kuryād yaṃ kāmayeta samānānāṃ śīreṣṭhaḥ syād itiPB  pavasva vāco agriya ity agram evainaṃ pariṇayatiPB  śrīr vai vāco graṃ śriyam evāsmin dadhātiPB  ete asṛgram indava iti bahubhyaḥ pratipadaṃ kuryātPB  eta iti sarvān evainān ṛddhyai bhūtyā abhivadati PB  eta iti vai prajāpatir devān asṛjatāsṛgram iti manuṣyān indava iti pitṝṃs tiraḥ pavitra iti grahān āśava iti stotraṃv viśvānīti  śastram abhi saubhagety anyāḥ prajāḥ PB  yad eta iti tasmād yāvanta evāgre devās tāvanta idānīmPB  sarvān vṛddhim ārdhnuvaṃ sthiteva hy eṣā vyāhṛtiḥPB  yad asṛgram iti tasmān manuṣyāḥ śvaḥśvaḥ sṛjyantePB  yad indava itīndava iva hi pitaraḥPB  mana ivaPB  yāntāḥ prajāḥ sṛṣṭā ṛddhim ārdhnuvaṃs tām ṛdhnuvanti yeṣām evaṃv vidvān etāṃ pratipadaṃ karotiPB  chandāṃsi vai somam āharaṃs taṃ gandharvo viśvāvasuḥ paryamuṣṇāt tenāpaḥprāviśat taṃ devatā anvaicchaṃs taṃ viṣṇur apsu paryapaśyat sa vyakāṅkṣad ayaṃ nūnā iti taṃ padā prāsphurat tasmāt pṛthag indavo sṛjyanta sa devatābhyo bhitastiṣṭhantībhya ete asṛgram indava iti prābravīd bahiṣpavamānena vai yajñaḥ sṛjyateyad ete asṛgram indava iti prastauti yajñam eva tat sṛṣṭaṃ devatābhyaḥ prāhaPB  vyṛddhaṃ vā etad apaśavyaṃ yat prātaḥsavanam aniḍaṃ hi yad iḍām asmabhyaṃ saṃyatam ity āha prātaḥsavanam eva tad iḍāvat paśumatPB  davidyūtatyā ruceti vrātāya pratipadaṃ kuryātPB  davidyūtatyā receti vai gāyatryā rūpaṃ pariṣṭobhantyeti triṣṭubhaḥ kṛpetyanuṣṭubhaḥ somāḥ śukrā gavāśira iti jagatyāḥ sarveṣāṃ vā eṣā cchandasāṃ rūpaṃ cchandāṃsīvakhalu vai vratopadeṣā pratipad bhavati svenaivaināṃs tad rūpeṇa samardhayatiPB  vṛddhā vā eta indriyeṇa vīryeṇa yad vrāta indriyaṃ vīryaṃ chandāṃsīndriyeṇaivainān vīryeṇa samardhayatiPB  agna āyūṃṣi pavasa iti pratipadaṃ kuryād yeṣāṃ dīkṣitānāṃ pramīyatePB  apūtā iva vā ete yeṣāṃ dīkṣitānāṃ pramīyate yady eṣāgnipāvamānī pratipad bhavaty agnir evainān niṣṭapati pavamānaḥ punātiPB  yad āyūṃṣīty āha ya eva jīvanti teṣv āyur dadhātiPB  ā no mitrāvaruṇeti jyogāmayāvine pratipadaṃ kuryātPB  apakrāntau vā etasya prāṇāpānau yasya jyog āmayati prāṇāpānau mitrāvaruṇau prāṇāpānāv evāsmin dadhātiPB  apaghnan pavate mṛdho pa somo arāvṇa ity anṛtam abhiśasyamānāya pratipadaṃ kuryātPB  arāvāṇo vā ete ye nṛtam abhiśaṃsanti tān evāsmād apahantiPB  gacchann indrasya niṣkṛtam iti pūtam evainaṃ yajñiyam indrasya niṣkṛtaṃ gamayatiPB  vṛṣā pavasva dhārayeti rājanyāya pratipadaṃ kuryād vṛṣā vai rājanyo vṛṣāṇam evainaṃ karotiPB  marutvate ca matsara iti maruto vai devānāṃ viśo viśam evāsmā anu niyunakty anapakrāmukāsmād viḍ bhavatiPB  viśvā dadhāna ojasety ojasaivāsmai vīryeṇa viśaṃ purastāt parigṛhṇāty anapakrāmukāsmād viḍ bhavatiPB  pavasvendo vṛṣāsuta iti pratipadaṃ kuryād yaḥ kāmayeta jane ma ṛdhyetetiPB  kṛdhī no yaśaso jana iti janatāyām evāsmā ṛdhyatePB  yuvaṃ hi sthaḥ svaḥ patī iti dvābhyāṃ pratipadaṃ kuryāt samāvadbhājāv evainau yajñasya karoty ubhau yajñayaśasenārpayatiPB  prāsya dhārā akṣarann iti vṛṣṭikāmāya pratipadaṃ kuryātPB  prāsya dhārā akṣarann iti divo vṛṣṭiṃ cyāvayati vṛṣṇaḥ sutasyaujasa ity antarikṣātPB  devāṃ anu prabhūṣata ity asmin loke pratiṣṭhāpayati PB  ojasā vā etad vīryeṇa pradīyate yad aprattaṃ bhavati yad vṛṣṇaḥ sutasyaujasa ity āhaujasaivāsmai vīryeṇa divo vṛṣṭiṃ prayacchati PB  tayā pavasva dhārayā yayā gāva ihāgamañ janyāsa up no gṛham iti pratipadaṃkuryād yaḥ kāmayetopa mā janyā gāvo nameyur vindeta me janyā gā rāṣṭram iti yad eṣāpratipad bhavaty upainaṃ janyā gāvo namanti vindate sya janyā gā rāṣṭramPB  ime vai lokā gāyatraṃ tryāvṛd geyaṃ trayo hīme lokā yat tryāvṛd gāyaty ebhir evainaṃ lokaiḥ saṃmimītePB  dvir avanarded dhiṅ kuryāt tṛtīyamPB  yat trir avanardaty ati tad gāyatraṃ recayatiPB  yo vai gāyatreṇāpratihṛtenodgāyaty apratiṣṭhāno bhavati hiṅkāro vai gāyatrasya pratihāraḥPB  sa manasā dhyeyaḥ pratihṛtena gāyatreṇodgāyati pratitiṣṭhatiPB  yo vā ebhyo lokebhyo gāyatraṃ gāyati naibhyo lokebhya āvṛścyata ima enaṃ lokā ūrjjābhisaṃvasatePB  mandram ivāgra ādadītātha tārataram atha tāratamaṃ tad ebhyo lokebhyo gāsītPB  aniruktaṃ geyam etad vai gāyatrasya krūraṃ yan niruktaṃ yad aniruktaṃ gāyati krūram evāsya parivṛṇaktiPB  prāṇo gāyatraṃ na vyavānyāt prāṇasyāvicchedāya yadi vyavāniti pramāyuko bhavati yadi na vyavāniti sarvam āyur etiPB  yadi vyavānyān madhya ṛco vyavānyāt prāṇo vai gāyatraṃ prāṇaḥ svaraḥ prāṇam eva tan madhyata ātman dadhāti sa sarvam āyur etiPB  iḍāṃ paśukāmāya nidhanaṃ kuryāt svaḥ svargakāmāya yaśo brahmavarcasakāmāyāyur āmayāvine haṃsīty abhicaratePB  ete vai gāyatrasya dohāḥPB  brahmavarcasasī paśumān bhavati ya evaṃv veda PB  prajāpatir devebhya ātmānaṃ yajñaṃ kṛtvā prāyacchat te nyo nyasmā agrāya nātiṣṭhanta tān abravīd ājim asminn iteti ta ājim āyan  yad ājim āyaṃs tad ājyānām ājyatvam PB  sa indro ved agnir vā idam agra ujjyeṣyatīti so bravīd yataro nāv idamagra ujjayat tan nau saheti so gnir agra udajayad atha mitrāvaruṇāv athendro thaiṣaikāhotrānujjitāsīt sa indro gnim abravīd yat sahāvocāvahī yan nau tad iti saiṣaindrāgnyadhyardham agne stotram adhyardham indrasyaPB  catvāri santi ṣaḍ devatyāniPB  ṣaḍdhā vihito yajño yāvān yajñas tam evārabhatePB  sarvāṇi svārāṇy ājyāni taj jāmi nānādevatyaiḥ stuvanty ajāmitāyai PB  grāmyebhyo vā etat paśubhyaḥ stuvanti yad ājyaiḥ punarabhyāvartaṃ stuvanti tasmāt parāñcaḥ prājyante pratyañcaḥ prajāyante tasmād  u pretya punar āyanti PB  etāvatā vāva mādhyandinaṃ savanaṃ pupuvePB  tribhiś ca cchandobhiḥ pañcabhiś ca sāmabhiḥPB  yan mādhyandinena pavamānena stuvanti mādhyandinam eva tat savanaṃ pāvayantiPB  etāvanti vāva sarvāṇi sāmāni yāvanti mādhyandine pavamānePB  gāyatraṃ nidhanavad anidhanam aiḍamPB  yan mādhyandinena pavamānena stuvanti sarvair eva tat sāmabhiḥ stuvantiPB  ātmā vai yajñasya pavamāno mukhaṃ gāyatrī prāṇo gāyatraṃ yad gāyatryāṃ gāyatreṇa stuvanti mukhata eva tat prāṇān dadhatiPB  prāṇāpānā vā etāni cchandāṃsi prāṇo gāyatrī vyāno bṛhaty apānas triṣṭub yad etaiś chandobhiḥ stuvanti prāṇāpānānām avicchedāya PB  ime vai lokā etāni cchandāṃsy ayam eva gāyatry ayaṃ madhyamo bṛhaty asāv uttamas triṣṭub yad etaś chandobhiḥ saṃhitaiḥ stuvanty  eṣāṃ lokānām avicchedāya PB  yad anyac chando ntarā vyaveyād imāṃl lokān vicchindyātPB  gāyatreṇa stutvā nidhanavatā stuvantīyaṃ vai gāyatry asyām eva tad āyatanaṃ kriyatePB  yad anidhanenāgre stuyur anāyatano yajamānaḥ syātPB  nidhanavatā stuvanti vīryaṃ vai gāyatrī vīryaṃ nidhanaṃ vīryeṇaiva tad vīryaṃ samardhayatiPB  aiḍena bṛhatīm ārabhantePB  paśavo vā iḍā paśavo bṛhatī paśuṣv eva tat paśūn dadhātiPB  bṛhatyāṃ bhūyiṣṭhāni sāmāni bhavantiPB  tatrāpi triṇidhanamPB  abaliṣṭha iva vā ayaṃ madhyami lokas tasyaiva tad āyatanaṃ kriyatePB  triṇidhanaṃ bhavati trīṇi savanānāṃ chidrāṇi tāni tenāpidhīyantePB  triṇidhanaṃ bhavati traya ime lokā eṣv eva lokeṣu pratitiṣṭhati PB  triṇidhanaṃ bhavaty etena vai mādhyandinaṃ savanaṃ pratiṣṭhitaṃ yat triṇidhanaṃ yat triṇidhanaṃ na syād apratiṣṭhitaṃ mādhyandinaṃ  savanaṃ syāt PB  dvyakṣarāṇi nidhanāni bhavanti dvipād yajamāno yajamānam eva yajñe paśuṣu pratiṣthāpayatiPB  anidhanam antato bhavati svargasya lokasyānatipādāyaPB  yan nidhanavat syād yajamānaṃ svargāl lokān nirhanyātPB  svāraṃ bhavatiPB  svareṇa vai devebhyo ntato nnādyaṃ pradīyate svareṇaiva tad devebhyo ntato nnādyaṃ prayacchatiPB  gāyatraṃ purastād bhavati svāram antataḥPB  prāṇo vai gāyatraṃ prāṇaḥ svaraḥ prāṇān evatad ubhayato dadhāti tasmād ubhayataḥ prāṇāḥ paśavaḥPB  yad gāyatraṃ purastād bhavati svāram antataḥ prāṇair eva praity apāne pratitiṣṭhatiPB  etad vai yajñasya svargyaṃ yan mādhyandinaṃ savanaṃ mādhyandinasya pavamānaḥpavamānasya bṛhatī yad bṛhatyāḥ stotre dakṣiṇā dīyante svargasyaiva tal lokasyāyatane dīyantePB  devā vai cchandāṃsy abruvan yuṣmābhiḥ svargyaṃl lokam ayāmeti te gāyatrīṃprāyuñjata tayā na vyāpnuvaṃs triṣṭubhaṃ prāyuñjata tayā na vyāpnuvañ jagatīṃ prāyuñjatatayā na vyāpnuvann anuṣṭubhaṃ prāyuñjata tayālpakādi na vyāpnuvaṃs ta āsāṃ diśāṃrasān prabṛhya catvāry akṣarāṇy upādadhuḥ sā bṛhaty abhavat tayemāṃl lokān vyāpnuvanPB  bṛhatī maryā yayemāṃl lokān vyāpāmeti tad bṛhatyā bṛhattvamPB  paśūn vā asyāntān upādadhuḥ paśavo vai bṛhatī yad bṛhatyāḥ stotre dakṣiṇā dīyante sva eva tad āyatane dīyantePB  yan nv ity āhur anyāni cchandāṃsi varṣīyāṃsi kasmād bṛhaty ucyata eṣāhīmāṃl lokān vyāpnon nānyac chandaḥ kiṃ cana yāni sapta caturuttarāṇi cchandāṃsitāni bṛhatīm abhisaṃpadyante tasmād bṛhaty ucyate PB  yan nv ity āhur gāyatraṃ prātaḥsavanaṃ traiṣṭubhaṃ mādhyandinaṃ savanaṃ jāgataṃ tṛtīyasavanaṃ kasmād bṛhatyā madhyandine stuvantīti PB  bahiṣpavamānena vai devā ādityaṃ svargaṃl lokam aharan sa nādhriyata taṃbṛhatyā madhyandine stabhnuvaṃs tasmād bṛhatyā madhyandinaṃ stuvanty ādityaṃ hyeṣā madhyandine dādhāraPB  yair u kaiś ca cchandobhir madhyandine stuvanti tāni triṣṭubham abhi saṃpadyante tasmāt triṣṭubho nayanti mādhyandināt savanātPB  prajāpatir akāmayata bahu syāṃ prajāyeyeti sa śocann amahīyamāno tiṣṭhatsa etad āmahīyavam apaśyat tenemāḥ prajā asṛjata tāḥ sṛṣṭā amahīyanta yad amahīyanta tasmād āmahīyavamPB  tā asmāt sṛṣṭā apākrāmaṃs tāsāṃ divi sad bhūmy ādada iti prāṇān ādattatā enaṃ prāṇeṣv ātteṣu punar upāvartanta tābhya ugraṃ śarma mahi śrava iti punaḥprāṇān prāyacchat tā asmād ud evāyodhaṃs tāsāṃ stauṣa iti manyūn avāśṛṇāt tato vaitasmai tāḥ śraiṣṭhyāyātiṣṭhantaPB  tiṣṭhante smai samānāḥ śraiṣṭhyāya ya evaṃv vedaPB  prajānāṃ ca vā eṣā sṛṣṭiḥ pāpavasīyaś ca vidhṛtir yad āmahīyavamPB  vidhṛtiḥ pāpavasīyaso bhavati ya evaṃv vedaPB  devā vai yaśaskāmāḥ sattram āsatāgnir indro vāyur makhas te bruvsn yanno yaśa ṛcchāt tan naḥ sahāsad iti teṣā makhaṃ yaśa ārcchat tad ādāyāpākrāmat tadasya prāsahāditsanta taṃ paryayatanta svadhanuḥ pratiṣṭhābhyātiṣṭhat tasya dhanurārtnirūrdhvā patitvā śiro cchinat sa pravargyo bhavad yajño vai makho yat pravargyaṃpravṛñjanti yajñasyaiva tac chiraḥ pratidadhatiPB  tad devā yaśo vyabhajanta tasyāgnī rauravaṃ prābṛhataPB  tad vai sa paśuvīryaṃ prābṛhata paśavo vai rauravamPB  paśumān bhavati ya evaṃv vedaPB  agnir vai rūras tasyaitad rauravam PB  asurā vai devān paryayatanta tata etāv agnī rūrau viṣvañcau stobhāv apaśyat tābhyām enān pratyauṣat te pratyuṣyamāṇā aravanta yad  aravanta tasmād rauravam PB  athendro yaudhājayaṃ prābṛhata tad vai sa vajraṃ prābṛhata vajro vai yaudhājayamPB  vajraṃ bhrātṛvyāya praharati ya evaṃv vedaPB  indro vai yudhājit tasyaitad yaudhājayamPB  yudhā maryā ajaiṣmeti tasmād yaudhājayamPB  atha vāyur auśanaṃ prābṛhataPB  tad vai sa prāṇvīryaṃ prābṛhata prāṇā vā auśanamPB  sarvam āyur eti ya evaṃv vedaPB  vāyur vā uśanaṃs tasyaitad auśanam PB  uśanā vai kāvyo surāṇāṃ purohita āsīt taṃ devāḥ kāmadughābhir apāmantrayanta tasmā etāny auśanāni prāyacchan kāmadughā vā auśanāni PB  kāmadughā enam upatiṣṭhante ya evaṃv vedaPB  prajāpatir akāmayata bahu syāṃ prajāyeyeti sa tūṣṇīṃ manasādhyāyat tasya yan manasy āsīt tad bṛhat samabhavatPB  sa ādadhīta garbho vai me yam antarhitas taṃv vācā prajanayā itiPB  sa vācaṃ vyasṛjata sā vāg rathantaram anvapadyataPB  ratham aryāḥ kṣeplātārīd iti tad rathantarasya rathantaratvamPB  tato bṛhad anu prājāyata bṛhan maryā idaṃ sa jyog antarabhūd iti tad bṛhato bṛhattvamPB  yathā vai putro jyeṣṭha evaṃ bṛhat prajāpateḥPB  jyeṣṭhabrāhmaṇaṃ vā etatPB  pra jyaiṣṭhyam āpnoti ya evaṃv vedaPB  yan nv ity āhur bṛhat pūrvaṃ prajāpatau samabhavat kasmād rathantaraṃ pūrvaṃ yogam ānaśa itiPB  bṛhad eva pūrvaṃ samabhavad rathantaraṃ tu pūrvaṃ sṛṣṭyāsṛjata tasmāt pūrvaṃ yogam ānaśe PB  tayoḥ samānaṃ nidhanam āsīt tasmin nātiṣṭhetāṃ ta ājim aitāṃ tayor has iti bṛhat prāṇam udajayad as iti rathantaram apānam abhisamaveṣṭata PB  prāṇāpānau vai bṛhadrathantare jyog āmayāvina ubhe kuryād apakrāntau vā etasya prāṇāpānau yasya jyog āmayati prāṇāpānāv evāsminPB  yan nv ity āhur ubhe bṛhadrathantare bahirṇidhane kasmād bṛhad bahirṇidhanāni bhajate ntarṇidhanāni rathantaram itiPB  prāṇo bṛhat tasmād bahirṇidhanāni bhajate bahir hi prāṇo pāno rathantaraṃ tasmād antarṇidhanāni bhajate ntar hy apānaḥPB  mahāvṛkṣau vai bṛhadrathantare nidhanena samarpyePB  yad vai mahāvṛkṣau samṛcchete bahu tatra vibhagnaṃ prabhagnaṃ śetePB  airaṃ vai bṛhad aiḍaṃ rathantaraṃ mano vai bṛhad vāg rathantaraṃ sāma vai bṛhad ṛg rathantaraṃ prāṇo vai bṛhad apāno rathantaram asau vai loko bṛhadayaṃ rathantaram etāni manasānvīkṣyodgāyet kḷptābhyām evābhyām udgāyatiPB  paśavo vai bṛhadrathantare aṣṭākṣareṇa prathamāyā ṛcaḥ prastauty aṣṭāśaphāṃs tat paśūn avarundhePB  dvyakṣareṇottarayor ṛcoḥ prastauti dvipād yajamāno yajamānam eva yajñe paśuṣu pratiṣṭhāpayatiPB  pañcākṣareṇa rathantarasya pratiharati pāṅktāṃs tat paśūn avarundhePB  caturakṣareṇa bṛhataḥ pratiharati catuṣpadas tat paśūn avarundhePB  na vai bṛhan na rathantaram ekaṃ chando yacchat tataḥ kakubhāv uttareupādadhus tasmād bṛhatī prathamā kakubhāv uttare tasmād bṛhadrathantare ekarcenakurvanti na hi te ekaṃ chando yacchatPB  nava bṛhato rohān rohati nava prāṇāḥ prāṇān evāvarundhePB  trīn prathamāyāṃ rohati bhūtaṃ bhavad bhaviṣyat tān evāvarundhe trīn madhyamāyāṃrohaty ātmānaṃ prajāṃ paśūṃs tān evāvarundhe trīn uttamāyāṃ rohati traya ime lokāeṣv eva lokeṣu pratitiṣṭhatiPB  sarvān kāmān avarundhe ya evaṃv vidvān bṛhato rohān rohati PB  vajreṇa vā etat prastotodgātāram abhipravartayati yad rathantaraṃ prastauti samudram antardhāyodgāyed vāg ity ādeyaṃv vāg vai samudraḥ  samudram evāntardadhāty ahiṃsāyai PB  balavad geyaṃ vajram evaṃ pravṛttaṃ pratyudgṛhṇātiPB  balvalā kurvatā geyam abhilobhayateva vajram evābhilobhayatiPB  kṣipraṃ geyaṃ svargasya lokasya samaṣṭyaiPB  devaratho vai rathantaram akṣareṇākṣareṇa pratiṣṭhāpayatodgeyam areṇāreṇa hi rathaḥ pratitiṣṭhatiPB  yo vai devaratham ananvālabhyātiṣṭhaty avāsmāt padyata iyaṃ vai devaratha imām ālabhyodgāyen nāsmād avapadyatePB  īśvaraṃ vai rathantaram udgātuś cakṣuḥ pramathitoḥ prastuyamāne saṃmīlet svardṛśaṃ prativīkṣeta nainaṃ cakṣur jahātiPB  prajananaṃ vai rathantaraṃ yat tasthuṣa ity āhāsthāyukodgātur vāg bhavatyapi prajananaṃ hanty asthuṣa iti vaktavyaṃ susthuṣa iti vā sthāyukodgātur vāg bhavatina prajananam api hantiPB  pṛṣṭhāni vā asṛjyanta tair devāḥ svargaṃl lokam āyaṃs teṣāṃ rathantaraṃ mahimnā nāśaknod utpatatPB  tasya vaśiṣṭho mahimno vinidhāya tena stutvā svargaṃl lokam ait tān saṃbhṛtyodgāyetPB  yas te goṣu mahimā yas te apsu rathe vā te stanayitnau ya u te yas te agnau mahimā tena saṃbhava rathantara draviṇavan na edhiPB  apo vā ṛtvyam ārcchat tāsāṃv vāyuḥ pṛṣṭhe vyavartata tato vasu vāmaṃ samabhavattasmin mitrāvaruṇau paryapaśyatāṃ tāv abrūtāṃv vāmaṃ maryā idaṃ deveṣv ājānīti tasmād vāmadevyam PB  tat parigṛhṇantāv tat pṛṣṭheṣu nyadadhuḥ sarvadevatyaṃ vai vāmadevyamPB  yat kavatīṣu tena prājāpatyaṃ ko hi prajāpatir yad aniruktāsu tena prājāpatyam anirukto hi prajāpatiḥPB  yad gāyatrīṣu tenāgneyaṃ gāyatracchandā hy agniḥPB  yat pṛṣṭheṣu nyadadadhus tenaindraṃ sarvāṇi hi pṛṣṭhānīndrasya niṣkevalyāniPB  yan maitrāvaruṇo nuśaṃsati tena maitrāvaruṇamPB  yad bahudevatyam uttamaṃ padaṃ tena vaiśvadevaṃ sarveṣv eva rūpeṣu pratitiṣṭhatiPB  prajāpatir vā etāṃ gāyatrīṃ yonim apaśyat sa ādīdhītāsmād yoneḥ pṛṣṭhāni sṛjā itiPB  sa rathantaram asṛjata tad rathasya ghoṣo nvasṛjyataPB  sa bṛhad asṛjata tat stanayitnor ghoṣo nvasṛjyata sa vairūpam asṛjata tad vā tasya ghoṣo nvasṛjyataPB  sa vairūpam asṛjata tad agner ghoṣo nvasṛjyataPB  sa śakvarīr asṛjata tad apāṃ ghoṣo nvasṛjyataPB  sa revatīr asṛjata tad gavāṃ ghoṣo nvasṛjyataPB  etair vā etāni saha ghoṣair asṛjyantaPB  sarve smin ghoṣāḥ sarvāḥ puṇyā vāco vadanti ya evaṃv vedaPB  pitā vai vāmadevyaṃ putrāḥ pṛṣṭhāniPB  etasmād vā etāni yoner asṛjyantaPB āsīt te devā yajñāyajñīyam apaśyaṃs teṣāṃ yajñāyajñāvo agnaya ity agnihotram avṛñjata girāgirā ca dakṣasa iti darśapūrṇamāsau prapravayam amṛtaṃ jātavedasam iti cāturmāsyāni priyaṃ mitraṃ na śaṃsiṣam yajñapathe pyastā yajñāyajñīyaṃ yad girāgirety āhātmānaṃ tad udgātā giratiPB  airaṃ kṛtvodgeyam irāyāṃ yajñaṃ pratiṣṭhāpayaty apramāyuka udgātā bhavatiPB  vaiśvānare vā etad udgātātmānaṃ pradadhāti yat prapra vayam ity āha praprīṃ vayam iti vaktavyaṃv vaiśvānaram eva parikrāmatiPB  yo vai nihnuvānaṃ cchanda upaiti pāpīyān ujjagivān bhavaty etad vai nihnuvānaṃcchando yan na śaṃsiṣam iti nu śaṃsiṣam iti vaktavyaṃ suśaṃsiṣam iti vā na nihnuvānaṃchanda upaiti vasīyān ujjagivān bhavatiPB  yasya vai yajñā vāgantā bhavanti vācaś chidreṇa sravanty ete vai yajñāvāgantā ye yajñāyajñīyāntā etad vācaś chidraṃ yad anṛtaṃ yad agniṣṭomayājy anṛtamāha tad anv asya yajñaḥ sravaty akṣareṇāntataḥ pratiṣṭhāpyam akṣareṇaiva yajñasyacchidram api dadhātiPB  virājo vā etad rūpaṃ yad akṣaraṃ virājy evāntataḥ pratitiṣṭhatiPB  ito vai prātar ūrdhvāṇi cchandāṃsi yujyante muto vāñci yajñāyajñīyasyastotre yujyante yajñā vo agnaye girā ca dakṣasa iti dvādaśākṣaraṃ pra vayam amṛtaṃjātavedasam ity ekādaśākṣaraṃ priyaṃ mitraṃn na śaṃsiṣam ity aṣṭākṣaramPB  anuṣṭubham uttamāṃ saṃpādayatīyaṃ vā anuṣṭub asyām eva pratitiṣṭhatiPB  vāg vā anuṣṭub vācy eva pratitiṣṭhati jyaiṣṭhyaṃ vā anuṣṭub jaiṣṭhya eva pratitiṣṭhatiPB  katham iva yajñāyajñīyaṃ geyam ity āhur yathānaḍvān prasrāvayamāṇa ittham iva cettham iva ceti PB  vaiśvānaraṃ vā etad udgātānu prasīdann etīty āhur yad yajñāyajñīyasyarcaṃ saṃpratyāheti parikrāmatevodgeyaṃv vaiśvānaram eva parikrāmati  PB  vaiśvānare vā etad adhvaryuḥ sadasyān abhisṛjati yad yajñāyajñīyasya stotram upāvartayati prāvṛtenodgeyaṃv vaiśvānareṇānabhidāhāya PB  na ha tu vai pitaraḥ prāvṛtaṃ jānanti yajñāyajñīyasya vai stotre pitaroyathāyathaṃ jijñāsanta ākarṇābhyāṃ prāvṛtyaṃ tad eva prāvṛtaṃ tad aprāvṛtaṃ jānantipitaro na vaiśvānaro hinastiPB  apaḥ paścāt patnya upasṛjanti vaiśvānaram eva tac chamayanty āpo hi śāntiḥPB  atho reta eva tat siñcanty āpo hi retaḥPB  dakṣiṇān ūrūn abhiṣiñcanti dakṣiṇato hi retaḥ sicyatePB  mahad iva pratyūhyaṃ mana evāsya taj janayantiPB  udgātrā patnīḥ saṃkhyāpayanti retodheyāyaPB  hiṅkāraṃ prati saṃkhyāpayanti hiṅkṛtād dhi reto dhīyataPB  ātṛtīyāyāḥ saṃkhyāpayanti trivad dhi retaḥPB  devā vā agniṣṭomam abhijityokthāni nāśaknuvann abhijetuṃ te gnim abruvaṃstvayā mukhenedaṃ cayāmeti so bravīt kiṃ me tataḥ syād iti yat kāmayasa ity abruvanso bravīn maddevatyāsūkthāni praṇayān itiPB  tasmād āgneyīṣūkthāni praṇayantiPB  tasmād u gāyatrīṣu gāyatracchandā hy agniḥPB  te gniṃ mukhaṃ kṛtvā sākam aśvenābhyakrāman yat sākam aśvenābhyakrāmaṃs tasmāt sākamaśvamPB  tasmāt sākamaśvenokthāni praṇayanty etena hi tāny agre bhyajayan PB  sa indro bravīt kaś cāhaṃ cedam anvavaiṣyāva ity ahaṃ ceti varuṇas taṃv varuṇo nvatiṣṭhad indra āharat tasmād aindrāvaruṇam anuśasyate PB  sa evābravīt kaś cāhaṃ cedam anvavaiṣyāva ity ahaṃ ceti bṛhaspatis taṃbṛhaspatir anvatiṣṭad indra āharat tasmād aindrābārhaspatyam anuśasyate sa evābravītkaś cāhaṃ cedam anvavaiṣyāva ity ahaṃ ceti viṣṇus taṃ viṣṇur anvatiṣṭad indra āharattasmād aindrāvaiṣṇavam anuśasyatePB  paśūn vā ebhyas tān āharat paśavo vā ukthāni paśukāma ukthena stuvīta paśumān bhavatiPB  bṛhatā vā indro vṛtrāya vajraṃ prāharat tasya tejaḥ parāpatat tat saubharam abhavatPB  jāmi vā etad yajñe kriyata ity āhur yad rathantaraṃ pṛṣṭhaṃ rathantaraṃsaṃdhir nāntarā bṛhatā stuvantīti yat saubhareṇa stuvanti bṛhataiva tad antarā stuvantibṛhato hy etat tejo yat saubharamPB  yadi bṛhat sāmātirātraḥ syāt saubharam ukthānāṃ brahma sāma kāryaṃ bṛhad eva tat tejasā samardhayatiPB  yadi rathantarasāmnā saubharaṃ kuryād ajāmitāyaiPB  devānāṃ vai svargaṃl lokaṃ yatāṃ diśo vlīyanta tāḥ saubhareṇo ity udastaṃbhuvaṃstato vai tā adṛṃhanta tataḥ pratyatiṣṭhaṃs tataḥ svargaṃl lokaṃ prājānan yaḥ svargakāmaḥsyād yaḥ pratiṣṭhākāmaḥ saubhareṇa stuvīta pra svargaṃl lokaṃ jānāti pratitṣṭhatiPB  prajāpatiḥ prajā asṛjata tāḥ sṛṣṭā āśanāyaṃs tābhyaḥ saubhareṇorg ity annaṃ prāyacchat tato vai tāḥ samaidhantaPB  samedhante tāṃ samāṃ prajā yatraivaṃv hīṣiti vṛṣṭikāmāya nidhanaṃ kuryād ūrg ity annādyakāmāyo iti svargakāmāyaPB  sarve vai kāmāḥ saubharaṃ sarveṣv eva kāmeṣu pratitiṣṭhatiPB  athaitan nārmedhamPB  nṛmedhasam āṅgirasaṃ sattram āsīnaṃ apahatyaiPB  pṛṣṭhāni vā asṛjyanta teṣāṃ yat tejo raso tyaricyata tad devāḥ samabharaṃs tad udvaṃśīyam abhavatPB  sarveṣāṃ vā etat pṛṣṭhānāṃ tejo yad udvaṃśīyaṃ tasmād vā etat purā sajātāya nākran gāyatrīṣu brahmavarcasakāmāyokthāni praṇayeyur gāyatryāṃ brahmasāmānuṣṭubhy acchāvākasāma saiṣā gāyatrī saṃpadyatePB  tejo brahmavarcasaṃ gāyatrī teja eva brahmavarcasam avarundhePB  gāyatrīṣu annādyam evāvarundhePB  akṣarapaṅktiṣu jyaiṣṭhyakāmāyokthāni praṇayeyur uṣṇihi brahmasāmānuṣṭubhy acchāvākasāma saiṣānuṣṭup saṃpadyatePB  jyaiṣṭhyaṃ vā anuṣṭub jyaiṣṭhyam avāvarundhePB  devā vā kutsaś ca luśaś cendraṃ vyahvayetāṃ sa indraḥ kutsam upāvartata taṃ śatenavārdhrībhir āṇḍayor abadhnāt taṃ luśo bhyavadat pramucyasva pari kutsād ihāgahikim u tvāvān āṇḍayor baddha āsātā iti tās vivasvad uṣasa iti sandhinā stuyuḥ prāṇā vai trivṛt stomānāṃ pratiṣṭhā rathantaraṃ sāmnāṃ prāṇāṃs caivopayanti pratiṣṭhāṃ ca PB  ṣaṣṭiṃ ca trīṇi ca śatāni hotā śaṃsatiPB  tāvatyaḥ saṃvatsarasya PB  yatra vā indrasya harī tad indraḥ indrasya vai harī bṛhadrathantare yad ubhe bṛhadrathantare bhavataḥ pūrva evendrasya harī ārabhante PB  tair aśravase kāryePB  turaśravasaś ca vai pārāvatānāṃ ca somau saṃsutāv āstāṃ tata ete turaśravāḥsāmanī apaśyat tābhyām asmā indraḥ śalmalināṃ yamunāyā havyaṃ nirāvahat yat tairaśravase bhavato havyam evaiṣāṃv vṛṅktePB  pūrve bhiṣuṇuyuḥPB  yā vai pūrvāḥ prasnānti tāḥ pūrvās tīrthaṃ jayanti pūrva evendram ārabhantePB  vihavyaṃ śasyam PB  jamadagneś ca vā ṛṣīṇāṃ ca somau saṃsutāv āstāṃ tata etaj gamadagnir vihavyam apaśyat tam indra upāvartata yad vihavyaṃ hotā śaṃsatīndram  evaiṣāṃv vṛṅkte  PB  yadītaro gniṣṭomaḥ syād ukthaḥ kāryo yady uktho tirātro yo vai bhūyān yajñakratuḥ sa indrasya priyo bhūyasaivaiṣāṃ yajnakratunendraṃv PB  atho khalv āhur duṣprāpa iva vai paraḥ panthā yam evāgre yajñakratum ārabheta tasmān neyād itiPB  sajanīyaṃ śasyam agastyasya kayāśubhīyaṃ śasyamPB  asyā amuṣyā adyaśvān mithunād ahorātrābhyām evainān nirbhajatiPB  yadi somam akrītam apahareyur anyaḥ kretavyaḥPB  yadi krītaṃ yo nyo bhyāśaṃ syāt sa āhṛtyaḥ somavikrayaṇe tu kiṃ cid dadyātPB  yadi somaṃ na vindeyuḥ pūtīkān abhiṣuṇuyur yadi na pūtīkān arjjunāniPB  gāyatrī somam āharat tasyā anu visṛjya somarakṣiḥ parṇam acchinat tasyayo ṃśuḥ parāpatat sa pūtīko bhavat tasmin devā ūtim avindann ūtīko vā eṣa yat pūtīkānabhiṣuṇvanty ūtim evāsmai vindantiPB  pratidhuk ca prātaḥ pūtīkāś ca śṛtaṃ ca madhyandine pūtīkāś ca dadhi cāparāhṇe pūtīkāś ca PB  somapītho vā etasmād apakrāmatīty āhur yasya somam apaharantīti sa oṣadhīś ca paśūṃś ca praviśati tam oṣadhibhyaś ca paśubhyaś cāvarundhe PB  indro vṛtram ahaṃs tasya yo nastaḥ somaḥ samadhāvat tāni babhrutūlānyarjunāni yo vapāyā utkhinnāyās tāni lohitatūlāni yāni babhrutūlāny arjunāni tānyabhiṣuṇuyād etad vai brahmaṇo rūpaṃ sākṣād eva somam abhiṣuṇotiPB  śrāyantīyaṃ brahmasāma kāryaṃ sad evainaṃ karotiPB  yajñāyajñīyam anuṣṭubhi prohed vācaivainaṃ samardhayati vāravantīyam agniṣṭomasāma kāryam indriyasya vīryasya parigṛhītyaiPB  pañca dakṣiṇā deyāḥPB  pāṅkto yajño yāvān yajñas tam evārabhatePB  avabhṛthād udetya punar dīkṣetaPB  tatra tad dadyād yad dāsyaṃ syātPB  yadi kalaśo dīryeta vaṣaṭkāraṇidhanaṃ brahmasāma kuryāt PB  avaṣaṭkṛto vā etasya somaḥ parāsicyate yasya kalaśo dīryate yad vaṣaṭkāraṇīdhanaṃ brahmasāma bhavati vaṣaṭkṛta evāsya somo bhavati PB  vidhuṃ dadrāṇaṃ samane bahūnām ity etāsu kāryamPB  eṣa hi bahūnāṃ samane dīryate yat kalaśaḥPB  tad āhur na vā ārtyārtir anūdyārtyā vā eṣa ārtim anuvadati yaḥ kalaśo dīrṇe dadrāṇavatīṣu karotītiPB  śrāyantīyam eva kāryam PB  prajāpatiḥ prajā asṛjata sa dugdho riricāno manyata sa etac chrāyantīyam apaśyat tenātmānaṃ samaśrīṇāt prajayā paśubhir indriyeṇa  PB  dugdha iva eṣa riricāno yasya kalaśo dīryate yac chrāyantīyaṃ brahmasāma bhavati punar evātmānaṃ saṃśrīṇāti prajayā paśubhir indriyeṇa PB  yadi śrāyantīyaṃ brahmasāma syād vaiṣṇavīṣv anuṣṭupsu vaṣaṭkāraṇidhanaṃ kuryātPB  yad vai yajñasya sravati vācaṃ pratisravati vāg anuṣṭup yajño viṣṇur vācaiva yajñasya cchidram apidadhātiPB  yad vai yajñasya sravaty antataḥ sravati vāravantīyam agniṣṭomasāma kāryaṃ yajñasyaiva cchidraṃ vārayatePB  yadi prātassavanāt somo tiricyeta asti somo ayaṃ suta iti marutvatīṣu gāyatreṣu stuyuḥPB  mādhyandinaṃ vā eṣa savanaṃ nikāmayamāno bhyatiricyate yaḥ prātassavanādatiricyate tasmān marutvatīṣu stuvanti marutvad dhi mādhyandinaṃ savanaṃ tasmād ugāyatrīṣu gāyatraṃ hi prātassavanamPB  yasmāt stomād atiricyate sa eva stomaḥ kāryaḥ salomatvāyaPB  aindrāvaiṣṇavaṃ hotānuśaṃsatiPB  vīryaṃ vā indro yajño viṣṇur vīrya eva yajñe pratitiṣṭhatiPB  yadi mādhyandināt savanād atiricyeta baṇ mahāṃ asi sūryety ādityavatīṣu gaurīvitena stuyuḥPB  tṛtīyasavanaṃ vā eṣa nikāmayamāno bhyatiricyate yo mādhyandināt savanādatiricyate tasmād ādityavatīṣu stuvanty ādityaṃ hi tṛtīyasavanaṃ tasmād u bṛhatīṣubārhataṃ hi mādhyandinaṃ savanam PB  yasmāt stomād atiricyeta sa eva stomaḥ kāryaḥ salomatvāyaindrāvaiṣṇavaṃ hotānuśaṃsati vīryaṃ vā indro yajño viṣṇur vīrya eva yajñe PB  yadi tṛtīyasavanād atiricyeta viṣṇoḥ śipiviṣṭavatīṣu gaurīvitena stuyuḥPB  yajño vai viṣṇuś śipiviṣṭo yajña eva viṣṇau pratitiṣṭhaty atiriktaṃ gaurīvitam atirikta evātiriktaṃ dadhātiPB  etad anyat kuryur ukthāni praṇayeyur ukthāni vā eṣa nikāmayamāno bhyatiricyateyo gniṣṭomād atiricyate yady ukthyebhyo tiricyetātirātraḥ kāryo rātriṃ vā eṣa nikāmayamānobhyatiricyate ya ukthyebhyo tiricyate yadi rātrer atiricyeta viṣṇoḥ śipiviṣṭavatīṣubṛhatā stuyur eṣu tu vā atiricyata ity āhur yo rātrer atiricyata itiPB  amuṃ vā eṣa lokaṃ nikāmayamāno bhyatiricyate yo rātrer atiricyate bṛhatā stuvanti bṛhad amuṃ lokam āptum arhati tam evāpnotiPB  yadi dīkṣitānāṃ pramīyate dagdhvāsthīny upanahya yo nediṣṭhī syāt taṃ dīkṣayitvā saha yajeranPB  etad anyat kuryur abhiṣutyānyat somam agṛhītvā grahān yāsau dakṣiṇā sraktis tad vā stuyur mārjālīye vāPB  api vā etasya yajñe yo dīkṣitaḥ pramīyate tam etena niravadayantePB  yāmena stuvanti yamalokam evainaṃ gamayantiPB  tisṛbhiḥ stuvanti tṛtīye hi loke pitaraḥPB  parācībhiḥ stuvanti parāṅ hīto sau lokaḥPB  sarparājñyā ṛgbhiḥ stuvantiPB  arbudaḥ sarpa etābhir mṛtāṃ tvacam apāhata mṛtām evaitābhis tvacam apaghnatePB  tā ṛco nubruvantas trir mārjālīyaṃ pariyanti savyān ūrūn āghnānāḥPB  stutam anuśaṃsaty amuṣminn evainaṃ loke nidhnuvantiPB  yanti vā ete patha ity āhur ye mṛtāya kurvantīty aindravāyavāgrān grahān gṛhṇate punaḥ panthānam apiyantiPB  agna āyūṃṣi pavasa iti pratipatkāryā ya eva jīvanti teṣv āyur dadhātiPB  saṃvatsare sthīni yājayeyuḥ saṃvvatsaro vai sarvasya śāntir yat purā saṃvvatsarād yājayeyur vācam aruṣkṛtāṃ krūrām ṛccheyuḥPB  vṛtaḥ pavamānāḥ syuḥ saptadaśam itarat sarvam PB  yat trivṛtaḥ pavamānā bhavanti prāṇā vai trivṛt prāṇān evopayanti yat saptadaśam itarat sarvaṃ prajāpatir vai saptadaśaḥ prajatim  PB  prāṇāpānair vā ete vyṛdhyanta ity āhur ye mṛtāya kurvantīti maitrāvaruṇāgrān grahān gṛhṇate prāṇāpānau mitrāvaruṇau prāṇāpānair  eva samṛdhyante PB  yasya kalaśa upadasyati kalaśam evāsyopadasyantaṃ prāṇo nūpadasyati prāṇo hi somaḥPB  tad āhuḥ payo vanayed itiPB  atho khalv āhur antarhitam iva vā etad yat payo hiraṇyam evāpobhyavanayed dhiraṇyam abhyunnayed itiPB  prāṇā vā āpo mṛtaṃ hiraṇyam amṛta evāsya prāṇān dadhāti sa sarvam āyur etiPB  yasya nārāśaṃsa upavāyati nārāśaṃsam evāsyopavāyantaṃ prāṇo nūpadasyati prāṇo hi somaḥPB  yam adhvaryur antato grahaṃ gṛhṇīyāt tasyāptum avanayetPB  prāyaścityai vai graho gṛhyate prāyaścityevāsmai prāyaścittiṃ karotiPB  yadi pītāpītau somau saṃgaccheyātām antaḥ paridhyaṅgārān nirvartya juhuyāt hutasya cāhutasya cāhutasya hutasya ca pītāpītasya somasyendrāgnī pibataṃ sutaṃ svāheti saiva tasya prāyaścittiḥPB  prajāpataye svāhety abhakṣaṇīyasya juhuyād uttarārdhyapūrvārdhya uparavaḥPB  indur indum avāgād ity avavṛṣṭasya bhakṣayetPB  tasya ta indrav indrapītasyendriyāvatas sarvagaṇasya sarvagaṇa upahūta upahūtasya bhakṣayāmiPB  hiraṇyagarbhaḥ samavartatāgra ity ājyenābhyupākṛtasya juhuyād agnīdhraṃparetya bhūtānāṃ jātaḥ patir eka āsīt sa dādhāra pṛthivīṃ dyām utemāṃ tasmai ta indohaviṣā vidhema svāheti saiva tasya prāyaścittiḥPB  yadi grāvāpi śīryate paśubhir yajamāno vyṛdhyate paśavo vai grāvāṇo dyutānasya mārutasya sāmnā stuyuḥPB  mārutā vai grāvāṇaḥ svenaivaināṃs tad rūpeṇa samardhayatiPB  yadi somam abhidahed grahān adhvaryuḥ spāśayeta stotrāṇy udgātā śastrāṇihotātha yathāpūrvaṃ yajñena careyuḥ pañca dakṣiṇā deyāḥ pāṅkto yajño yāvān yajñastam ārabhate vabhṛthād udetya punar dīkṣate tatra tad dadyād yad dāsyaṃ syāt purādvādaśyā dīkṣeta yad dvādaśīm atinayed antardhīyetaPB  yadi mahāvīro bhidyeta taṃ bhinnam abhimṛśed ya ṛte cid abhiśriṣaḥ purā jatrubhya ātṛdaḥ saṃdhātā saṃdhiṃ maghavā purūvasur niṣkartā vihrutaṃ punaḥ mā bhema niṣṭyā ivendra tvad araṇā iva vanāni na prajahitāny adrivo duroṣāso amanmahi amanmahīd anāśavo nugrābhaś ca vṛtrahan sakṛt sute mahatā śūra rādhasānu stomaṃ mademahīti mahāvīraṃ bhinnam abhimṛśet saiva tasya prāyaścittiḥ PB  asuryaṃ vā etasmād varṇaṃ kṛtvā teja indriyaṃ vīryam annādyaṃ prajāḥ paśavo pakrāmanti yasya yūpo virohati sa īśvaraḥ pāpīyān PB  tvāṣṭraṃ paśuṃ bahurūpam ālabheta tvaṣṭā vai paśūnāṃ rūpāṇāṃ vikartātam eva tad upadhāvati sa enaṃ tejaseindriyeṇa vīryeṇānnādyena prajayā paśubhiḥ punassamardhayati saiva tasya prāyaścittiḥPB  agninā pṛthivyauṣadhibhis tenāyaṃ lokas trivṛd vāyunāntarikṣeṇa vayobhistenaiṣa lokās trivṛd yo yam antar ādityena divā nakṣatrais tenāsau lokas trivṛdetad eva trivṛta āyatanam eṣāsya bandhutāPB  āyatanavān bandhumān bhavati ya evaṃv vedaPB  tam u pratiṣṭhetyāhus trivṛd dhy evaiṣu lokeṣu pratiṣṭhitaḥPB  ardhamāsa eva pañcadaśasyāyatanam eṣāsya bandhutāPB  āyatanavān bandhumān bhavati ya evaṃv vedaPB  taṃ caujo balam ity āhur ardhamāsaśo hi prajāḥ paśava ojo balaṃ puṣyantiPB  saṃvatsara eva saptadaśasyāyatanaṃ dvādaśa māsāḥ pañcadartava etad eva saptadaśasyāyatanam eṣāsya bandhutāPB  āyatanavān bandhumān bhavati ya evaṃv vedaPB  tam u prajāpatir ity āhuḥ saṃvatsaraṃ hi prajāḥ paśavo nuprajāyante PB  āditya evaikaviṃsasyāyatanaṃ dvādaśa māsāḥ pañcavartas traya ime lokā asāv āditya ekaviṃśa etad evaikaviṃśasyāyatanam eṣāsya bandhutā PB  āyatanavān bandhumān bhavati ya evaṃv vedaPB  tam u devatalpa ity āhuḥ pra devatalpam āpnoti ya evaṃv vedaPB  trivṛd eva triṇavasyāyatanam eṣāsya bandhutāPB  āyatanavān bandhumān bhavati ya evaṃv vedaPB  tam u puṣṭir ity āhus trivṛd dhy evaiṣa puṣṭaḥPB  devatā eva trayastriṃśasyāyatanaṃ trayastriṃśad devatāḥ prajāpatiś catustriṃśa etad eva trayastriṃśasyāyatanam eṣāsya bandhutāPB  āyatanavān bandhumān bhavati ya evaṃv vedaPB  tam u nāka ity āhur na hi prajāpatiḥ kasmai canākamPB  chandāṃsy eva chandomānām āyatanam eṣaiṣāṃ bandhutāPB  āyatanavān bandhumān bhavati ya evaṃv vedaPB  tān u puṣṭir ity āhuḥ paśavo hi chandomāḥPB  prajāpatiḥ prajā asṛjata so tāmyat tasmai vāj jyotir udagṛhṇāt so bravītko me yaṃ jyotir udagṛhṇād iti svaiva te vāg ity abravīt tām abravīd virājaṃ tvācchandasāṃ jyotiṣkṛtvā yajāntā itiPB  tasmād yo virājaṃ stomaṃ saṃpadyate taṃ jyotiṣṭomo gniṣṭoma ity ācakṣate virāḍ ḍhi chandasāṃ jyotiḥPB  jyotiḥ samānānāṃ bhavati ya evaṃv veda PB  anuṣṭup ca vai saptadaśaś ca samabhavatāṃ sānuṣṭup caturuttarāṇi chandāṃsy asṛjata ṣaḍuttarān stomān saptadaśas tāv etān madhyataḥ PB  trivṛc ca triṇavaś ca rāthantarau tāv ajaś cāśvaś cānvasṛjyetāṃ tasmāt tau rāthantaraṃ prācīnaṃ pradhūnutaḥPB  pañcadaśaś caikaviṃśaś ca bārhatau tau gauś cāviś cānvasṛjyetāṃ tasmāt tau bārhataṃ prācīnaṃ bhāskurutaḥPB  evaṃ vai vidvāṃsam āhur api grāmyāṇāṃ paśūnāṃ vāca ājānātiPB  prajāpatir akāmayata bahu syāṃ prajāyeyeti sa ātmann ṛtvyam apaśyat tataṛtvijo sṛjata yad ṛtvyād asṛjata tad ṛtvijām ṛtviktvaṃ tair etaṃ dvādaśāham upāsīdat so rādhnotPB  pitā no rātsīd iti māsā upāsīdaṃs te dīkṣayaivārādhnuvann upasatsu trayodaśamadīkṣayan so  nuvyam abhavat tasmād upasatsu didīkṣāṇo nuvyaṃ bhavaty eva ca hitrayodaśaṃ māsaṃ cakṣate naiva ca PB  eko dīkṣetaiko hi prajāpatir arādhnod dvādaśa dīkṣeran dvādaśa hi māsā arādhnuvaṃś caturviṃśatir dīkṣeraṃś caturviṃśatir hy ardhamāsā  PB  yadi pañcadaśo dīkṣeteme pañceme pañceme pañceme pañceme catvāro sāv eka iti nirdiśeyur yasmā arāddhikāmāḥ syus tam evārāddhir  anveti sarva itare rādhnuvanti PB  yo vai devānāṃ gṛhapatiṃ vedāśnute gārhapataṃ pra gārhapatam āpnotiPB  saṃvatsaro vai devānāṃ gṛhapatiḥ sa eva prajāpatis tasya māsā eva saha dīkṣiṇaḥPB  vindate saha dīkṣiṇo śnute gārhapatyaṃ pra gārhapatyaṃ āpnoti ya evaṃv veda  PB  yo vai chandasāṃ svarājaṃ vedāśnute svārājyaṃ pra svārājyaṃ āpnoti bṛhatī vāva chandasāṃ svarāḍ aśnute svārājyaṃ pra svārājyaṃ  āpnoti ya evaṃv veda  PB  tām etām annādyāya vyāvṛjyāsate yad etaṃ dvādaśāhaṃ dvādaśa dīkṣā svādaśopasado dvādaśa prasutaḥ ṣaṭriṃśad etā rātrayo bhavanti  ṣaṭtriṃśadakṣarā bṛhatī PB  jāyate vāva dīkṣayā punīta upasadbhir devalokam eva sutyayāpyetiPB  etāvad vāva saṃvatsara indriyaṃ vīryaṃ yad etā rātrayo dvādaśa pūṛnamāsyodvādaśaikaṣṭakā dvādaśāmāvāsyā yāvad eva saṃvatsara indriyaṃ vīryaṃ tad etenāptvāvarundhe dvādaśāhenaPB  triṃśadakṣarā vā eṣā virāḍ ṣaḍ ṛtava ṛtuṣv eva virājā pratitiṣṭhaty ṛtubhir virāji PB  dvātriṃśadakṣarā vā eṣānuṣṭub vāg anuṣṭup catuṣpādaḥ paśavo vācā paśūn dādhāra tasmād vācā siddhā vācāhūtā āyanti tasmād u nāma  PB  bhūtaṃ pūrvo tirātro bhaviṣyad uttaraḥ pṛthivī pūrvo tirātro dyaur uttaro gniḥ pūrvo tirātra āditya uttaraḥ prāṇaḥ pūrvo tirātra  udāna uttaraḥ PB  cakṣuṣī atirātrau kanīnike agniṣṭomau yasmād antarā agniṣṭomāv atirātrābhyāṃ tasmād antare satyau kanīnike bhuṅktaḥPB  saṃvatsarasya vā etau daṃṣṭrau yad atirātrau tayor na svaptavyaṃ saṃvatsarasya daṃṣṭrayor ātmānaṃ ned apidadhānītiPB  tad āhuḥ ko svaptum arhati yad vāva prāṇo jāgāra tad eva jāgaritam iti PB  gāyatrīṃ vā etāṃ jyotiḥpakṣām āsate yad etaṃ dvādaśāham aṣṭau madhya ukthā agniṣṭomāv abhito māsā svargṃ lokam etyājarasaṃ brahmādyam  annam atti dīpyamānaḥ PB  triṣpurastād rathantaraṃ upayanti tryāvṛd vai vāk sarvām eva vācam avarudhya sarvam annādyaṃ dvādaśāhaṃ tanvate PB  jāmi vā etad yajñe kriyata ity āhur yat triṣpurastād rathantaram upayantīti saubharam ukthānāṃ brahmasāma bhavati tenaiva tad ajāmi PB  pratnavatyaḥ prāyaṇīyasyāhnaḥ pratipado bhavanti teno eva tad ajāmiPB  trir vevopariṣṭād rathantaram upayanti trāvṛd vai vāk sarvām eva vācam avarudhya sarvam annādyaṃ dvādaśāhād uttiṣṭhantiPB  trayo vā ete trirātrā yad eṣa dvādaśāho gāytramukhaḥ prathamo gāyatramadhyo dvitīyo gāyatrottamas tṛtīyaḥPB  yasmād gāyatramukhaḥ prathamas tasmād ūrdhvo gnir dīdāya yasmād gāyatramadhyo dvitīyas tasmāt tiryaṅ vāyuḥ pavatePB PB PB  tejasā vā ete prayanti tejo madhye dadhati tejo bhyudyanti jyotiṣā vāete prayanti jyotir madhye dadhati jyotir abhyudyanti cakṣuṣā vā ete prayanti cakṣurmadhye dadhati cakṣur abhyudyanti prāṇena vā ete prayanti prāṇaṃ madhye dadhati prāṇamabhyudyanti ye gāyatryā prayanti gāyatrīṃ madhye dadhati gāyatrim abhyudyantiPB  tantraṃ vā etad vitāyate yad eṣa dvādaśāhas tasyetair mayūkhā yad gāyatry asaṃvyāthāyaPB  girikṣidauccāmanyaveti hovācābhipratārī kākṣaseniḥ kathaṃ dvādaśāha itiyathārān nemiḥ paryety evam enaṃ gāyatrī paryeti avisraṃsāya yathārā nābhau dhṛtāevam asyāṃ dvādaśāho dhṛtaḥPB  anuṣṭubhaṃ vā etām annādyāya vyāvṛjyāsate yad etaṃ dvādaśāhamPB  aṣṭābhir vā akṣair anuṣṭup prathamaṃ dvādaśāhasyāhar duyacchaty ekādaśabhir dvitīyaṃ dvādaśābhis tṛtīyamPB  akṣaraṃ tryakṣaram ucchiṣyate tad evottaraṃ trirātram anuvidadhātiPB  chandāṃsy evāsyās tṛtīyaṃ trirātraṃ vahantiPB  tāṃ vā etāṃ pratīcīṃ tiraścīṃ parācīm āsate nnādyāya tasmāt pratyañcaṃ tiryañcaṃ parāñcaṃ prajāḥ paśum upajīvantiPB  chandāṃsi vā anyonyasya lokam abhadhyāyan gāyatrī triṣṭubhas triṣṭubjagatyā jagatī gāyatryās tāni vyauhan yathālokaṃ tato vai tāni yaṃyaṃ kāmam akāmayanta tam asanvanPB  yatkāmo vyūḍhacchandasā dvadaśāhena yajate so smai kāmaḥ samṛdhyate PB  oko vai devānāṃ dvādaśāho yatho vai manuṣyā imaṃ lokam āviṣṭā evaṃ devatā dvādaśāham āviṣṭā devatā ha vā etena yajate ya evaṃv  vidvān dvādaśāhena yajate PB  gṛhā vai devānāṃ dvādaśāho nāgṛhatāyā bhayyamPB  yo vai dvādaśāham agniṣṭomena kalpamānaṃ veda kalpate smai prātaḥsavanenaivaprathamas trirātraḥ kalpate mādhyandinena dvitīyas tṛtīyasavanena tṛtīyo gniṣṭomasāmnaivadaśamam ahaḥ kalpatePB  kalpate smai ya evaṃv veda PB  eti prety āśumad vītimad rukmat tejasvad yuñjānaṃ prathamasyāhno rūpaṃ trivṛtaḥ stomasya gāyatrasya chandaso rathantarasya sāmnaḥ PB  vṛṣavad vṛtravad rayimad viśvavad upasthitaṃ dvitīyasyāhno rūpaṃ pañcadaśasya stomasya traiṣṭubhasya chandaso bṛhataḥ sāmnaḥPB  udvat trivad digvat gomaṭ ṭaṣabhavat tṛtīyasyāhno rūpaṃ saptadaśasya stomasya jāgatasya chandaso vairūpasya sāmnaḥPB  rājanvaj janavadvat sūryavad virāḍanutodavac caturthasyāhno rūpam ekaviṃśasya stomasyānuṣṭubhasya chandaso rājasya vai sāmnaḥ PB  citravac chiśumat paṅktiḥ śakvarī dyūnākṣarā gomad ṛṣabhavad vajryabhimat pañcamasyāhno rūpaṃ triṇavasya stomasya pāṅktena chandaso  śakvarīṇāṃ sāmnaḥ  PB  parivat prativat saptapadā dvipadā vinārāśaṃsā gomad ṛṣabhavat ṣaṣṭhasyāhno rūpaṃ trayastriṃśasya stomasya sarveṣāṃ chandasāṃ rūpaṃ revatīnāṃ sāmnaḥPB  yasmād eṣā samānā satī ṣaḍahavibhaktir nānārūpā tasmād virūpaḥ saṃvvatsaraḥPB  virūpam enam anuprajāyate ya evaṃv vedaPB  agna iti prathamasyāhno rūpam agnivibhakter agnim iti dvitīyasyāgnineti tṛtīyasyāgnir iti caturthasyaPB  devā vai śriyam aicchaṃs tān na prathame hany avindan na dvitīye natṛtīye tāñ caturthe hany avindan vindate śriyaṃ ya evaṃ vedāgner iti pañcamasyateno śrīḥ pratyupoditety āhuḥPB  aprativādy enaṃ bhrātṛvyo bhavati ya evaṃ vedaPB  agna iti ṣaṣṭhasya yenaiva rūpeṇa prayanti tad abhyudyantiPB  yasmād eṣā samānā saty agnivbhaktir nānārūpā tasmād yathartv ādityas tapatiPB  indreti prathamasyāhno rūpam indravibhakter indram iti dvitīyasyendreṇetitṛtīyasyendra iti caturthasyendrād iti pañcamasyendreti ṣaṣṭhasya yenaiva rūpeṇaprayanti tad abhyudyanti yasmād eṣā samānā satīndravibhaktir nānārūpā tasmād yathartv oṣadhayaḥ pacyantePB  yad ṛcā prastauti tat prathamasyāhno rūpam svaravibhakter yat purastātstobhaṃ tad dvitīyasya yad ubhayataḥ stobhaṃ tat tṛtīyasya yad anutunnaṃ tac caturthasyayad abhyārabdhaṃ tat pañcamasya yad ihakāreṇābhyastaṃ tat ṣaṣṭhasyāhno rūpamPB  svarāṇāṃ yasmād eṣā samānā satī svaravibhaktir nnānārūpā tasmād yathartu vāyuḥ pavatePB  padanidhanaṃ prathamasyāhno rūpam nidhanavibhakter bahirṇidhanaṃ dvitīyasyaniṃnidhanaṃ tṛtīyasyenidhanañ caturthasyāthakāraṇidhanaṃ pañcamasya yad ihākāreṇābhyastaṃtat ṣaṣṭhasyāhno rūpaṃ nidhanānāṃ yasmād eṣā samānā satī nidhanavibhaktir nnānārūpātasmād ime lokāḥ saha santo nānaivaPB  dravadiḍaṃ prathamasyāhno rūpam iḍāvibhakter ūrdhveḍaṃ dvitīyasya pariṣṭubdheḍaṃtṛtīyasyeḍābhir aiḍaṃ caturthasyādhyardheḍaṃ pañcamasya yad ihākāreṇābhyastaṃ tatṣaṣṭhasyāhno rūpam iḍānāṃ yasmād eṣā samānā satīḍāvibhaktir nnānārūpā tasmāt samānāḥsantaḥ paśavo nānārūpāḥPB  bharadvājāyanā vai sattram āsata tān apṛcchan kiṃ prathamenāhnā kurutetipraivaimeti kiṃ dvitīyenety avasam evākurmahīti kiṃ tṛtīyeneti pary evāplavāmahītikiṃ caturtheneti sataiva sad apyadadhmeti kiṃ pañcameneti prāṇān eva vicchindantaaimeti kiṃ ṣaṣṭhenetīdam evāgacchāmeti itiPB  yasya padena prastauty atha svāram abhi vāva tena devāḥ paśūn apaśyanyat purastāt stobhaṃ atha svāram ud eva tenāsṛjanata yad ubhayataḥ stobham atha svāramebhya eva tena lokebhyo devāḥ paśubhyo nnādyaṃ prāyacchan yad anutunnam atha svāramupaiva tenāśikṣan yasya madhye nidhanam atha svāraṃ garbhāṃs tenādadhata tāni havatāsvāreṇa prājanayanPB  imaṃ vāva devā lokaṃ padanidhanenābhy ajayann amuṃ bahirṇidhanenāntarikṣaṃdiṅnidhanenāmṛtatvam īnidhanenāgacchan brahmavarcasam athanidhanenāvārundhatāsminneva loka ihanidhanena pratyatiṣṭhanPB  imaṃ vāva devā lokaṃ dravadiḍenābhy ajayann amum ūrdhveḍenāntarikṣaṃpariṣṭubdheḍena pratiṣṭhām iḍābhir aiḍenāvārundhata pratiṣṭhāyādhyardheḍena vyajayantāsminneva loka iheḍena pratyatiṣṭhanPB  na vāk saṃvatsaram ativadatīḍaiva saṃvatsaram ativadati garbheṇa saṃvatsare paryāvṛtya prajāyete tenātivadatiPB  tā vā etāś catasraḥ ṣaḍahaṃ parācya iḍā atiyanty eṣā nūtaiṣā viṣūcy eṣā pratīcy etad vīḍamPB  saṃvatsaro gnir vāk samvatsaro yad agnir vibhajyate vācam eva tad vibhajantiPB  dve dve akṣare vibhajanti dvau dvau hi māsāv ṛturatho māsānām eva tad rūpaṃ kriyate PB  ṣaḍ ahāni vibhajanti ṣaḍ ṛtava ṛtūnāṃ dhṛtyā ṛtūnāṃ pratiṣṭhityā atho ṛtūnām eva tad rūpaṃ kriyate ṣaḍ u puruṣā yān agnir anuvihriyate PB  yad idaṃ bahudhāgnir vihriyate tad asāv ādityaḥ sarvāḥ prajāḥ pratyaṅ tasmād ete devate vibhaktim ānaśāte nāto nyā kā canaPB  stomo yujyate sattriyebhyo  harbhyaḥ pratnavatībhiś copavatībhiś caPB  yat pratnavatyo upavatībhyaḥ pūrvā yujyante brahma tat pūrvaṃ kṣatrād yujyate brahma hi pūrvaṃ kṣatramPB  manas tat pūrvaṃ vāco yujyate mano hi yad dhi manasābhigacchati tad vācā vadatiPB  bṛhat tat pūrvaṃ rathantarād yujyate bṛhad dhi pūrvaṃ rathantarād vijityā tu vai rathantaraṃ pūrvaṃ yogam ānaśePB  sambhāryās tṛcā bhavanti yathāśiṣṭhān vahiṣṭhān sambhared evam evaitān sambharanti gatyai PB  nava bhavanti navāhasya yuktyā ṛcarcaivāhar yunakti yathāprārthasya śamyā avadadhyād evam evaitan navāhasya śamyā avadadhāti gatyai PB  trivṛd eva stomo bhavati tejase brahmavarcasāyaPB  ubhābhyāṃ vai rūpābhyāṃ bahiṣpavamānyo yujyante yatsāmā stomo bhavati tad ājyeṣuPB  nirāhāvanty ājyāni bhavanti yuktam eva tair āhvayatiPB  agna āyāhi vītaya ā no mitrāvaruṇāyāhi suṣamā hi ta indrāgnī āgataṃ sutam iti rāthantaram eva tad rūpaṃ nirdyotayati stomaḥ itiPB  pra somāso vipaścita iti gāyatrī bhavati pretyā abhidroṇāni babhravaity abhikrāntyai stutā indrāya vāyava iti saṃskṛtyai pra soma deva vītaya iti pretyaipra tu draveti pretyai pra vā etenāhnā yantiPB  gāyatraṃ bhavatiPB  yad eva gāyatrasya brāhmaṇamPB  āśvaṃ bhavatiPB  aśvo vai bhūtvā prajāpatiḥ prajā asṛjata sa prājāyata bahur abhavat prajāyate bahur bhavaty āśvena tuṣṭuvānaḥPB  ekākṣaraṃ nidhanam upayanti rathantarasyānativādāyaPB  anativādy enaṃ bhrātṛvyo bhavati ya evaṃ vedaPB  somasāma bhavatiPB  yathā vā imā anyā oṣadhayaḥ evaṃ soma āsīt sa tapo tapyata sa etat somasāmāpaśyattena rājyamādhipatyam agacchad yaśo bhavad rājyam ādhipatyaṃ gacchati yaśo bhavatisomasāmnā tuṣṭuvānaḥPB  yaudhājayaṃ bhavati yad eva yaudhājayasya brāhmaṇamPB  auśanaṃ yad auśanasya stomaḥPB  abhi tvā śūra no nu ma ity abhīti rathantarasya rūpaṃ rathantaraṃ hy etad ahaḥPB  kayā naś citra ābhuvad iti kavatyas tena prājāpatyāḥ ko hi prajāpatiḥ prajāpater āptyai PB  taṃ vo dasmam ṛtīṣahaṃ vasor mandānam andhaso bhivatsaṃ na svasareṣu dhenava ity abhīti rathantarasya rūpaṃ rathantaraṃ hy etad PB  indraṃ gīrbhir havāmaha iti havanta evainam PB  tarobhir vo vidadvasum iti stomo vai taro yajño vidadvasuḥ stomena vai yajño yujyate yat tarobhir vo vidadvasum ity āha yajñam  eva tad yunakti PB  rathantaraṃ bhavati brahma vai rathantaraṃ brahma prāyaṇīyam ahar brahmaṇa eva tad brahmākramya prayantiPB  iyaṃ vai rathantaram asyām eva pratiṣṭhāya sattram āsate PB  vāmadevyaṃ bhavati paśavo vai vāmadevyaṃ paśūnām avaruddhyai prājāpatyaṃ vai vāmadevyaṃ prajāpatāv eva pratiṣṭhāya sattram āsate PB  naudhasaṃ bhavati brahma vai naudhasaṃ brahma prāyaṇīyam ahar brahmaṇa eva tad rahmākramante PB  kāleyaṃ bhavati samānaloke vai kāleyañ ca rathantarañ ceyaṃ vai rathantaraṃ paśavaḥ kāleyam asyāñ caiva paśuṣu ca pratiṣṭhāya PB  dravadiḍaṃ tathā hy etasyāhno rūpaṃ stomaḥPB  pra somāso madacyuta iti gāyatrī bhavati madavad vai rasavṛt tṛtīyasavanaṃmadam eva tad rasaṃ dadhāty ayā pasvasva devayur ity eti rathantarasya rūpaṃ rāthantaraṃhy etad ahaḥ pavate har yato harir iti bṛhato rūpaṃ bṛhad eva tad etasminn ahaniyunakti tad yuktaṃ śva ārabhante pra sunvānāyāndhasa iti pravatyo bhavanti praṇinīṇyamiva hy etad ahar abhi priyāṇi pavate ca nohita ity abhīti rathantarasya rūpaṃ rāthantaraṃ hy etad ahaḥPB  yajñā yajñā vo agnaya ity agner vai yajño yajña eva tad yajñaṃ pratiṣṭhāpayatiPB  gāyatraṃ bhavati yad eva gāyatrasya brāhmaṇamPB  saṃhitaṃ bhavati vyakṣaraṇidhanaṃ pratiṣṭhāyai pratiṣṭhāyaiva sattram āsatePB  saphaṃ bhavatiPB  saphena vai devā imān lokān samāpnuvvan yat samāpnuvaṃs tat saphasya saphatvam imān evaitena lokān samāpya sattram āsatePB  ākṣāraṃ bhavatiPB  aṣṭau vā etāḥ kādughā āsaṃs tāsām ekā samaśīryata sā kṛṣir abhavad ṛdhyate smai kṛṣau ya evaṃ vedaPB  tāsu devāsurā aspardhanta te devā asurān kāmadughābhya ākṣāreṇānudanta nudate bhrātṛvyaṃ kāmadughābhya ākṣāreṇa tuṣṭuvānaḥPB  ebhyo vai lokebhyo raso pākrāmat taṃ prajāpatir ākṣāreṇākṣārayad yad ākṣārayat tad ākṣārasyākṣāratvamPB  tasmād yaḥ purā puṇyo bhūtvā paścāt pāpīyān syād ākṣāraṃ brahma sāma kurvītātmany eved indriyaṃ vīryaṃ rasam ākṣārayatiPB  januṣaikarco bhavato hno dhṛtyai yad vā etasyāhno dhṛtaṃ tad etābhyāṃ dādhāraPB  gaurīvitaṃ bhavatiPB  gaurīvitir vā etac chāktyo brāhmaṇo tiriktam apaśyat tad gaurīvitam abhavatPB  atiriktaṃ vā etad atiriktena stuvanti yad gaurīvitenāhīnāñ chavastanavad bhavaty api prajāyā upakḷptamPB  vṛṣā vā etad vājisāma vṛṣabho retodhā adya stuvanti śvaḥ prajāyatePB  anuṣṭubhi chandasāṃ kriyate nuṣṭub bhi chandasāṃ yoniḥ svāyām eva tad yonau reto dhatte prajātyaiPB  prajāyate bahur bhavati ya evaṃ veda PB  dvyudāsaṃ bhavaty etau vā udāsau svargasya lokasyāvasānadarśau pūrveṇa pūrvam ahaḥ saṃsthāpayanty uttareṇottaram ahar abhyativadanti PB  tad yathādaḥ pūrvedyuḥ spaṣṭaṃ tṛṇodakam anvavasyanto yanty evam eva tābhyāṃ svargaṃ lokam anvavasyanto yantiPB  gautamaṃ bhavatiPB  sāmārṣeyavat svargāya yujyate svargāl lokān na cyavate tuṣṭuvānaḥPB  yad u caivānuṣtṭubhasya madhye nidhanasya brāhmaṇaṃ tad du caitasyaPB  kāvaṃ bhavatiPB  lokabinduḥ sāma vindate lokaṃ kāvena tuṣṭuvānaḥPB  svārasu svareṇa svareṇa hi devebhyo ntato nnādyaṃ pradīyate svareṇaiva tad devebhyo ntato nnādyaṃ pra yacchatiPB  yajñāyajñīyaṃ bhavatiPB  vāg yajñāyajñīyaṃ vāci yajñaḥ pratiṣṭhito vācy eva tad yajñam antataḥ pratiṣṭhāpayanti taṃ vāco dhi śva ārabhantePB  trivṛd eva stomo bhavati tejase brahmavarcasāyaPB  pratipad bhavatiPB  samārabhate dvirātrasyāvrisraṃsāyaPB  pavasvendo vṛṣāsuta ity anurūpyo bhavati vṛṣāvad vā eta aindraṃ traiṣṭubham ahar yat dvitīyaṃ tad eva tad abhivadatiPB  pūrvam u tad rūpam apareṇa rūpeṇānuvadati yat pūrvaṃ rūpam apareṇa rūpeṇānuvadati tad anurūpasyānurūpatvamPB  anurūpa enaṃ putro jāyate ya evaṃ vedaPB  stotrīyānurūpau tṛcau bhavataḥ prāṇāpānānām avarudhyaiPB  vṛṣaṇvantas tṛcā bhavatīndriyasya vīryasyāvarudhyaiPB  tṛca uttamo bhavatiPB  yenaiva prāṇena prayanti tam abhyudyantiPB  pañdadaśa eva stomo bhavatiPB  ojasy eva tad vīrye pratitiṣṭhati ojo vīryaṃ pañcadaśaḥPB  ubhābhyāṃ vai rūpābhyāṃ bahiṣpavamānyo yujyante yatsāmā stomo bhavati tad ājyeṣuPB  nirāhopasthitāny ājyāni bhavanti PB  agniṃ dūtaṃ vṛṇīmahe mitraṃ vayaṃ havāmaha indram id gāthino bṛhad indro agnā namo bṛhad iti bārhatam eva tad rūpaṃ nirdyotayati PB  vṛṣā pavasva dhārayeti gāyatrī bhavaty ahno dhṛtyaiPB  vṛṣaṇvatyas triṣṭubho rūpeṇa traiṣṭubhaṃ hy etad ahaḥPB  punānas soma dhārayeti dhṛtyaiPB  vṛṣā śoṇo abhikanikradad gā itiPB  vṛṣaṇvatyas triṣṭubho rūpeṇa samṛddhā vṛṣaṇvad vā etad aindraṃ traiṣṭubham ahar yat dvitīyaṃ tad eva tad abhivadatiPB  gāyatraṃ bhavati yad eva gāyatrasya brāhmaṇamPB  yauktāśvaṃ bhavatiPB  yuktāśvo va āṅgirasaḥ śiśū jātau viparyaharat tasmān mantro pākrāmatsa tapo tapyata sa etad yauktāśvam apaśyat taṃ mantra upāvartata tad vāva sa tarhyakāmayata kāmasani sama yauktāśvaṃ kāmam evaitenāvarundhePB  āyāsye bhavataḥ PB  ayāsyo vā āṅgirasa ādityānāṃ dīkṣitānām annādyam āśnāt taṃ śug ārcchat sa tapo tapyata sa ete āyāsye apaśyat tābhyāṃ śucam apāhatāpa  śucaṃ hata āyāsyābhyāṃ tuṣṭuvānaḥ PB  ebhyo vai lokebhyo vṛṣṭir apākrāmat tām ayāsya āyāsyābhyām acyāvayat cyāvayati vṛṣṭim āyāsyābhyāṃ tuṣṭuvānaḥPB  annādyaṃ vāva tad ebhyo lokebhyo pākrāmat tad ayāsya āyāsyābhyām acyāvayat cyāvayaty annādyam āyāsyābhyāṃ tuṣṭuvānaḥPB  vāsiṣṭhaṃ bhavati PB  vasiṣṭho vā etena vaiḍavaḥ stutvāñjasā svargaṃ lokam apaśyat svargasya lokasyānukhyātyai svargāl lokān na cyavate tuṣṭuvānaḥ stomaḥ PB  tvām id dhi havāmaha iti tvam iti bṛhato rūpaṃ bārhataṃ hy etad ahaḥPB  abhipravaḥ surādhasam iti yuñjate vai pūrveṇāhnā hy etena prayantiPB  tvām idā hyo nara ity adya caiva hyaś ca samārabhate dvirātrasyāvisraṃsāyaPB  bṛhad bhavati varṣma vai bṛhad varṣma dvitīyam ahar varṣmaṇa eva tad varṣmākramantePB  śyetaṃ bhavati sāmnorvāho yajñasya santatyaiPB  mādhucchandasaṃ bhavati sāmārṣeyavat svargāya yujyate svargāl lokān na cyavate tuṣṭuvānaḥPB  ūrdhveḍaṃ tathā hy etasyāhno rūpaṃ stomaḥPB  yas te mado vareṇya iti gāyatrī bhavatiPB  madavad vai rasavat tṛtīyasavanaṃ madam eva tad rasaṃ dadhātiPB  pavasva madhumattama iti pavanta iva hy etenāhnā madhumattama ity annaṃ vai madhv annādyam eva tad yajamāne dadhātiPB  indram accha sutā ima itīndriyasya vīryasyāvarudhyaiPB  ayaṃ pūṣā rayir bhaga itiPB  anuṣṭubhaḥ satyas triṣṭubho rūpeṇa traiṣṭubhaṃ hy etad ahaḥPB  vṛṣāmatīnāṃ pavate vicakṣaṇa iti jagatyaḥ satyas triṣṭubho rūpeṇa traiṣṭubhaṃ hy etad ahaḥPB  gāyatraṃ bhavati yad eva gāyatrasya brāhmaṇamPB  hāviṣmataṃ bhavatiPB  haviṣmāṃś ca vai haviṣkṛc cāṅgirasāv āstāṃ dvitīye hani haviṣmān arādhnon navame hani haviṣkṛtPB  ayaṃ haviṣmān ity eva jātam ahar jātaṃ somaṃ prāha devebhyaḥ sāmnaivāsmā āśiṣam āśāste sāma hi saty āśīḥPB  śaṅku bhavaty ahno dhṛtyai yad vā adhṛtaṃ śaṅkunā tad dādhāra PB  tad u sīdantīyam iy āhur etena vai prajāpatir ūrdhva imān lokān asīdad yad asīdat tat sīdantīyasya sīdantīyatvam svargasya lokasya samaṣṭyaiPB  gaurīvitaṃ bhavati yad eva gaurīvitasya brāhmaṇamPB  krauñcaṃ bhavatiPB  vāg vai krauñcaṃ vāg dvādaśāho vācy eva tad vācā stuvate yajñasya prabhūtyaiPB  yāmaṃ bhavatiPB ukthāny adhyajayann etenābhyakrāmanPB  āmahīyavaṃ bhavati kḷptiś cānnādyañ ca samānaṃ vadantīṣu kriyata idam ittham asad itiPB  kṣatraṃ vā etad ahar abhinirvadati yat pañcadaśaṃ yad gāyatrīṣu brahmasāmabhavati brahma caiva tat kṣatrañ ca sayujī karoti brahmaiva kṣatrasya purastān nidadhatibrahmaṇe kṣatrañ ca viśañ cānuge karotiPB  brahma vai pūrvam ahaḥ kṣatraṃ dvitīyaṃ yad gāyatrīṣu bhavatiPB  davidyutatī vai gāyatrī pariṣṭobhantī triṣṭub gavāśīr jagatī trīṇi rūpāṇi samārabhate trirātrasyāvisraṃsāyaPB  ete asṛgram indava ity anurūpo bhavatiPB  eta iti vai prajāpatir devān putro jāyate ya evaṃ veda PB  stotrīyānurūpau tṛco bhavataḥ prāṇāpānānām avarudhyaiPB  rājā medhābhir īyate pavamāno manāv adhy antarikṣeṇa yātava itiPB  antarikṣadevatyas tṛco bhavaty abhi somāsa āyava itiPB  abhīti rathantarasya rūpaṃ bṛhad iti bṛhata ubhayoḥ saha rūpam upaity ubhau hi varṇāv etad ahaḥPB  tisro vāca īrayati pravahnir iti tṛtīyasyāhno rūpaṃ tena tṛtīyam ahar ārabhantePB  triṣṭubhaḥ satyo jagatyo rūpeṇa jāgataṃ hy etad ahaḥPB  gāyatraṃ bhavati yad eva gāyatrasya brāhmaṇamPB  vaiṣṭambhaṃ bhavatiPB  ahar vā etad avlīyata tad devā vaiṣṭambhair vyaṣṭabhnuvaṃs apa pāpmānaṃ hate paurūmadgena  PB  devāś ca vāsurāś cāspardhanta te devā asurāṇāṃ paurūmadgena puro majjayan yat puro majjayaṃs tasmāt paurūmadgaṃ pāpmānam evaitena  bhrātṛvyaṃ majjayati PB  gautamaṃ hārivarṇaṃ bhavatiPB  indraś ca vai namuciś cāsuraḥ samadadhātāṃ na no naktan na divāhanannārdreṇa na śuṣkeṇeti tasya vyuṣṭāyām anudita āditye pāṃ phenena śiro chinad etadvai na naktaṃ na divā yat viṣṭabhnoti bhūyaso nnādyasyāvarudhyaiPB  vairājaṃ sāma bhavati virāṭsu stuvanti vairājā viṣṭambhāḥ samīcīr virājo dadhāty annādyāyaPB  anutunnaṃ gāyati retodheyāyānutunnād dhi reto dhīyatePB  dakṣiṇa ūrāv udgatur agniṃ manthanti dakṣiṇato hi retaḥ sicyatePB  upākṛte hiṅkṛte manthanti jātam abhihiṅkarotiPB  tasmāj jātaṃ putraṃ paśavo bhihiṅkurvantiPB  tasmai jātāyāmīmāṃsanta gārhapatye praharāmā āgnīdhrā āhavanīyā itiPB  āhavanīye praharanty etad āyatano vai yajamāno yadā havanīye svam eva tad āyatanaṃ jyotiṣmat karotiPB  jyotiṣmān brahmavarcasī bhavati ya evaṃ vedaPB  abhijuhoti śāntyaiPB  ājyenābhijuhoti tejo vā ājyaṃ teja eva tad ātman dhattePB  preddho agne dīdihi puro na iti virājābhijuhoty annaṃ virāḍ annādyasyāvarudhyaiPB  traiśokaṃ brahmasāma bhavatiPB  atijagatīṣu stuvanty ahna utkrāntyā ud vā etenāhnā krāmantiPB  diveti nidhanam upayanti pāpmano pahatyā apapāpmānaṃ hate traiśokena tuṣṭuvānaḥPB  bhāradvājasya pṛśny achāvākasāma bhavatiPB  annaṃ vai devāḥ pṛśnīti vadanty annādyasyāvarudhyaiPB  iḍābhir aiḍaṃ tathā hy etasyāhno rūpaṃ stomaḥPB  paripriyā divaḥ kavir iti parivatyo bhavanty anto vai caturtham ahas tasyaitāḥ paryāptyaiPB  tvaṃ hy aṅga daivyeti tvam iti bṛhato rūpaṃ bārhataṃ hy etad ahaḥPB  somaḥ punāna ūrmiṇā vyaṃvāraṃ vidhāvatiagre vācaḥ pavamānaḥ kanikradad itiPB  agraṃ hy etarhi vāco gacchann agram evaitayā yajamānaṃ gamayantiPB  puro jitīvo andhasā iti virājau vairājaṃ hy etad ahaḥPB  somaḥ pavate janitā matīnām iti prātassavane ṣoḍaśinaṃ gṛhītaṃ taṃ tṛtīyasavane prajanayantiPB  triṣṭubhaḥ satyo jagatyo rūpeṇa tasmāj jagatīnāṃ loke kriyantePB  gāyatraṃ bhavati yad eva gāyatrasya brāhmaṇamPB  aurṇāyavaṃ bhavatiPB  aṅgiraso vai sattram āsata teṣām āptaḥ spṛtaḥ svargo loka āsīt panthānaṃtu devayānaṃ na prājānaṃs teṣāṃ kalyāṇa āṅgiraso dhyāyam udavrajat sa ūrṇāyuṃ gandharvamapsarasāṃ madhye preṅkhayamāṇam upait sa iyām iti yāṃ yām abhyadiśat sainam akāmayatatam abhyavadat kālyāṇā ity āso vai vaḥ spṛtaḥ svargo lokaḥ panthānaṃ tu devayānaṃna prajānīthedaṃ sāma svargyaṃ lokam eṣy atha mā tu vocoham adarśam itiPB  sa ait kalyāṇaḥ so bravīd āpto vai naḥ spṛtaḥ svargo lokaḥ panthānaṃtu devayānaṃ prajānīma idaṃ sāma svargyaṃ tena stutvā svargaṃ lokam eṣyāma iti kaste vocad ity aham evādarśam iti tena stutvā svargaṃ lokam āyann ahīyata kalyāṇonṛtaṃ hi so vadat sa eṣaḥ śvitraḥPB  svargyaṃ vā etat sāma svargalokaḥ puṇyaloko bhavaty aurṇāyavena tuṣṭuvānaḥPB  bṛhatkaṃ bhavatiPB  sāmārṣeyeṇa praśastaṃ tvaṃ hīty annādyasyāvarudhyai hīti vā annaṃ pradīyate ṣoḍaśinam u caivaitenodyacchatiPB  ātīṣādīyaṃ bhavatiPB  āyur vā ātīṣādīyam āyuṣo ṣarudhyaiPB  ātamitor nidhanam upayanty āyur eva sarvam āpnuvantiPB  nānadaṃ bhavatiPB  jyāyo bhyārambham atihāya pañcam ahaḥ ṣaṣṭhasyāhna ārambhas tena ṣaṣṭham ahar ārabhante santatyaiPB  ṣoḍaśākṣareṇa prastauti ṣoḍaśinam u caivaitenodyacchatiPB  āndhīgavaṃ bhavatiPB  kayor annādyam avarūndha āndhīgavena tuṣṭuvānaḥPB  vātsapraṃ bhavatiPB  etasmin vai vairājaṃ pratiṣṭhitaṃ pratitiṣṭhati vātsapreṇa tuṣṭuvānaḥ PB  vatsaprīr bhālandanaḥ śraddhāṃ nāvindata sa tapo tapyata sa etad vātsapram apaśyat sa śraddhām avindata śraddhā vindāmahā iti  vai sattram āsate vindate śraddhām PB  īnidhanaṃ tathā hy etasyāhno rūpaṃ nidhanāntāḥ pavamānā bhavanty ahno dhṛtyai stomaḥPB  agniṃ vo vṛdhantam itiPB  avardhanta hy etarhi yajamānam eva tathā vardhayantiPB  vayam u tvām apūrvya ity apūrvāṃ hy etarhi prajāpates tanūm agacchann apūrvam evaitayā yajamānaṃ gamayanti PB  imam indra sutaṃ piba jyeṣṭham amartyaṃ madam iti jyaiṣṭhaṃ hy etarhi vāco gacchan jyaiṣṭhyam evaitayā yajamānaṃ gamayanti PB  saindhukṣitaṃ bhavati PB  sindhukṣid vai rājanyarṣir jyog aparuddhaś caran sa etat saindhukṣitam apaśyat so vāgacchat pratyatiṣṭhad avagacchati pratitiṣṭhati  saindhukṣitena tuṣṭuvānaḥ PB  saubharaṃ bhavati bṛhatas tejaḥPB  pannam iva vai caturtham ahas tad etena bṛhatas tejasottabhnoti saubhareṇaPB  vasiṣṭhasya priyaṃ bhavatiPB  etena vai vasiṣṭha indrasya premāṇam agacchat premāṇaṃ devatānāṃ gacchati vāsiṣṭhena tuṣṭuvānaḥ stomaḥPB  indraś ca bṛhac ca samabhavatāṃ tam indraṃ bṛhad ekayā tanvāty aricyatatasyā abibhedanayā mābhibhaviṣyatīti so bravīt ṣoḍaśī te yaṃ yajñakratur astv itisa ṣoḍaśy abhavat tad asya janmaPB  atiśriyā bhrātṛvyaṃ ricyate yo gāyatrīṣu dvipadāsu bṛhatā ṣoḍaśinā stutePB  upa no haribhiḥ stutam ity etā vai gāyatryo dvipadā etāsu stotavyam PB  indraḥ prajāpatim upādhāvad vṛtraṃ hanānīti tasmā etām anuṣṭubham apaharasaṃ prāyacchat tayā nāstṛṇuta yad astṛtā vyanadat tan  nānadasya nānadatvam PB  taṃ punar upādhāvat tasmai saptānāṃ hotrāṇāṃ haro nirmāya prāyacchat tam astṛṇutaPB  stṛṇute taṃ yaṃ tustūrṣate ya evaṃ vedaPB  tasmād dharivatīṣu stuvanti harivatīḥ śaṃsanti harivatīṣu graho gṛhyate haro hy asmai nirmāya prāyacchatPB  ekaviṃśāyatano vā eṣa yat ṣoḍaśī sapta hi prātassavane hotrā vaṣaṭkurvanti sapta mādhyandine savane sapta tṛtīyasavanePB  gaurīvitaṃ bhavatiPB  gaurīvitir vā etac chāktyo brahmaṇo tiriktam apaśyat tad gaurīvitamabhavad atiriktaṃ etad atiriktena stuvanti yad gaurīvitena ṣoḍaśinaṃ śvastanavānbhavaty api prajāyā upakḷptaḥ PB  viśālaṃ libjayā śrūtyābhyadhād iti hovācopoditir gopāleyo nuṣṭubhi nānadam akar gaurīvitena ṣoḍaśinam astoṣṭāñjasā śriyam upāgān  na śriyā avapadyata iti  PB  eṣa vai viśālaṃ libjayā bhūtyābhidadhāti yo nuṣṭubhi nānadaṃ kṛtvā gaurīvitena ṣoḍaśinā stute ñjasā śriyam upaiti na śriyā PB  śakvarīṣu ṣoḍaśinā stuvīta yaḥ kāmayeta vajrī syām itiPB  vajro vai ṣoḍaśī vajraḥ śakvaryo vajreṇaivāsmai vajraṃ spṛṇoti vajrī bhavatiPB  anuṣṭupsu ṣoḍaśinā stuvīta yaḥ kāmayeta na mā vāg ativadetPB  vajro vai ṣoḍaśī vāg anuṣṭub vajreṇaivāsmai vācaṃ spṛṇoti nainaṃ vāg ativadatiPB  asāvi soma indra ta ity etāsu stotavyamPB  virāṭsv annādyakāmaḥ ṣoḍaśinā stuvīta vajro vai ṣoḍaśī vairājam annaṃ vajreṇaivāsmā annaṃ spṛṇoty annādo bhavatiPB  pra vo mahe vṛdhe bharadhvam ity etāsu stotavyamPB  trayastriṃśadakṣarā vā etā virājo yad ekaviṃśatiḥ pratiṣṭhā sā yad dvādaśa prajātiḥ sāPB  pratiṣṭhāya prajāyate no cāntasthāyāṃ jīryate ya evaṃ vedaPB  atha vā etā ekapadās tryakṣarā viṣṇoś chando bhurijaḥ śakvaryaḥPB  etābhir vā indro vṛtram ahan kṣipraṃ vā etābhiḥ pāpmānaṃ hanti kṣipraṃ vasīyān bhavatiPB  catustriṃśadakṣarāḥ saṃstuto bhavati trayastriṃśaddevattāḥ prajāpatiś catustriṃśo devatānāṃ prajāpatim evopayanty ariṣṭyaiPB  hiraṇyaṃ sampradāyaṃ ṣoḍaśinā stuvate jyotiṣmān asya ṣoḍaśī bhavatiPB  aśvaḥ kṛṣṇa upatiṣṭhati sāmyekṣayāya bhrātṛvyalokam eva sa vidhamaṃs tiṣṭhatiPB  ekākṣaraṃ vai devānām avamaṃ chanda āsīt saptākṣaraṃ paramaṃ navākṣaramasurāṇām avamaṃ chanda āsīt pañcadaśākṣaraṃ paramaṃ devāś ca vā asurāś cāspardhantatān prajāpatir ānuṣṭubho bhūtvāntarātiṣṭhat taṃ devāsurā vyahvayanta sa devān upāvartatatato devā abhavan parāsurāḥPB  bhavaty ātmanā parāsya bhrātṛvyo bhavati ya evaṃ vedaPB  te devā asurāṇām ekākṣareṇaiva pañcadaśākṣaram avṛñjata dvyakṣareṇacaturdaśākṣaraṃ tryakṣareṇa trayodaśākṣaraṃ caturakṣareṇa dvādaśākṣaraṃ pañcākṣareṇaikādaśākṣaraṃṣaḍakṣareṇa daśākṣaraṃ saptākṣareṇa navākṣaram aṣṭābhir evāṣṭāv avṛñjataPB  evam eva bhrātṛvyād bhūtiṃ vṛṅkte ya evaṃ veda PB  aparuddhayajña iva vā eṣa yat ṣoḍaśī kanīyasvina iva vai tarhi devā āsan bhūyasvino surāḥ kanīyasvina bhūyasvinaṃ bhrātṛvyaṃ  vṛṅkte ya evaṃ veda PB  yasmād anyo na paro sti jāto ya ābabhūva bhuvanāni viśvāprajāpatiḥ prajayā samvidānas trīṇi jyotīṃ ṣi sacate sa ṣoḍaśī ity udgātā graham avekṣatePB  jyotiṣmān asya ṣoḍaśī bhavati ya evaṃ vedaPB  ekaviṃśa eva stomo bhavati pratiṣṭhāyai pratitiṣṭhatiPB  govit pavasva vasuvid dhiraṇyavid iti pañcamasyāhnaḥ pratipad bhavatiPB  govid vā etad vasuvid dhiraṇyavidyac chakvaryaḥPB  paśavaś śakvaryaḥ sarvaṃ paśubhir vindatePB  tvaṃ suvīro asi somaviśvavid ity eṣa yāva suvīro yasya paśavas tad eva tad abhivadatiPB  tās te kṣarantu madhumad ghṛtaṃ paya iti madhumad vai ghṛtaṃ payaḥ paśavaḥ kṣaranti tad eva tad abhivadatiPB  pavamānasya viśvavid ity anurūpo bhavatiPB  viśvam eva tadvit tam abhivadati viśvaṃ hi paśubhir vindatePB  pra te sargā asṛkṣata iti sṛṣṭānīva hy etarhy ahāniPB  pūrvam u caiva tad rūpam apareṇa rūpeṇānuvadati yat pūrvaṃ rūpeṇānuvadati tad anurūpasyānurūpatvamanurūpa enaṃ putro jāyate ya evaṃ veda stotrīyānurupau tṛcau bhavataḥ prāṇāpānānām avarudhyaiPB  saptarcau bhavataḥ chandasāṃ dhṛtyaiPB  caturṛco bhavati pratiṣṭhāyaiPB  tṛca uttamo bhavati yenaiva prāṇena prayanti tam abhy udyantiPB  triṇava eva stomo bhavati pratiṣṭhāyai puṣṭyai trivṛd vā eṣa puṣṭaḥPB  tava śriyo varṣasy eva vidyuta ity āgneyam ājyaṃ bhavatiPB  śrīr vai paśavaḥ śrīḥ śakvaryaḥ tad eva tad abhivadatiPB  agneś cikitra uṣasām ivetaya itītānīva hy etarhy ahānītiPB  ā te yatente rathyo yathā pṛthag ity eva hy etarhy ahāni yatantePB  purūruṇā cid dhy asty avo nūnaṃ vāṃ varuṇa iti maitrāvaruṇamPB  yad vai yajñasya duriṣṭaṃ tad varuṇo gṛhṇāti tad eva tad avayajatiPB  uttiṣṭhann ojasā saha ity aindramPB  pañca vā ṛtava utthānasya rūpam ojasā sahety ojasaiva vīryeṇa sahottiṣṭhantiPB  indrāgnī yuvām ima iti rāthantaram aindrāgnamPB  rathantaram etat parokṣaṃ yac chakvaryo rāthantaram eva tad rūpaṃ nirdyotayati stomaḥPB  arṣā soma dyumattama iti viṣṇumatyo gāyatryo bhavantiPB  brahma vai gāyatrī yajño viṣṇur brahmaṇy eva tad yajñaṃ pratiṣṭhāpayatiPB  soma uṣvāṇas sotṛbhir iti simānāṃ rūpaṃ svenaivaitās tad rūpeṇa samardhayatiPB  yat soma citram ukthyam iti gāyatryaḥ satyas triṣṭubho rūpeṇa tasmāt triṣṭubhāṃ loke kriyantePB  gāyatraṃ bhavati yad eva gāyatrasya brāhmaṇamPB  yaṇvaṃ bhavati paśavo vai yaṇvaṃ paśūnām avarudhyaiPB  santataṃ gāyati yajñasya santatyePB  adhyardheḍaṃ tathā hy etasyāhno rūpamPB  śākalaṃ bhavatiPB  etena vai śakalaḥ pañcame hani pratyatiṣṭhat pratitiṣṭhati śākalena tuṣṭuvānaḥPB  vārśaṃ bhavatiPB  vṛśo vaijānas tryaruṇasya traidhātavasyaikṣvākasya purohita āsīt saaikṣvāko dhāvayat brāhmaṇakumāraṃ rathena vyacchinat sa purohitam abravīt tava māpurodhāyām idam īdṛg upāgād iti tam etena sāmnā samairayat tad vāva sa tarhy akāmayatakāmasani sāma vārśaṃ kāmam evaitenāvarundhePB  adhyardheḍaṃ tathā hy etasyāhno rūpamPB  mānavaṃ bhavatiPB  etena vai manuḥ prajāpatiṃ bhūmānam agacchat prajāyate bahur bhavati mānavena tuṣṭuvānaḥPB  ānūpaṃ bhavatiPB  etena vai vadhryaśva ānūpaḥ paśūnāṃ bhūmānam āśnuta paśūnāṃ bhūmānam aśnuta ānūpena tuṣṭuvānaḥPB  vāmraṃ bhavatiPB  māmārṣeyeṇa praśastaṃ yaṃ vai gām aśvaṃ puruṣaṃ praśaṃsanti vāma iti taṃ praśaṃsanty ahar evaitena praśaṃsantiPB  adhyardheḍaṃ tathā hy etasyāhno rūpamPB  triṇidhanam āgneyaṃ bhavati pratiṣṭhāyai PB  agriḥ sṛṣṭo nodadīpyata taṃ prajāpatir etena sāmnopādhamat sa udadīpyata dīptiś ca vā etat sāma brahmavarcasaṃ ca dīptiś caivaitena  brahmavarcasaṃ cāvarundhe PB  śaiśavaṃ bhavatiPB  śiśur vā āṅgiraso mantrakṛtāṃ mantrakṛd āsīt sa pitṛn putrakā ity āmantrayatataṃ pitaro bruvan na dharmaṃ karoṣi yo naḥ pitṛn sataḥ putrakā ity āmantrayama itiso bravīd ahaṃ vāva vaḥ pitāsmi yo mantrakṛd asmītitaṃ deveṣv apṛcchanta te devā abuvann eṣa vāva pitā yo mantrakṛd iti tad vai sa udajayad ujjayati śaiśavena tuṣṭuvānaḥPB  gāyatrīṣu stuvanti pratiṣṭhāyai brahmavarcasāya yenaiva prāṇena prayanti tam abhyudyantiPB  viṣṇumatyo gāyatryo bhavanti tad u traiṣṭubhād rūpān na yanti stomaḥPB  indraḥ prajāpatim upādhāvad vṛtraṃ hanānīti tasmā etac chandobhya indriyaṃvīryaṃ nirmāya prāyacchad etena śaknuhīti tac chakvarīṇāṃ śakvarītvaṃ sīmānam abhinattat simā mahnyam akarot tan mahnyā mahān ghoṣa āsīt tan mahānāmnyaḥPB  diśaḥ pañcapadā dādhārartūn ṣaṭpadā chandāṃsi saptapadā puruṣaṃ dvipadāPB  dvyopaśāḥ saṃstutā bhavanti tasmād dvyopaśāḥ paśavaḥPB  iḍe abhito thakāraṃ tasmāc chṛṅge tīkṣṇīyasī stūpātPB  upakṣudrā gāyati tasmād upakṣudrāḥ paśavaḥPB  aṃsaśliṣṭā gāyati tasmād asaṃśliṣṭāḥ paśavaḥPB  nānārūpā gāyati tasmān nānārūpāḥ paśavaḥPB  āpo vai kṣīrarasā āsaṃste devāḥ pāpavasīyasād abibhayur yad apa upanidhāya stuvate pāpavasīyaso vidhṛtyaiPB  vidhṛtiḥ pāpavasīyaso bhavati ya evaṃ vedaPB  gāyatram ayanaṃ bhavati brahmavarcasakāmasya svarṇidhanaṃ madhunāmuṣmiṃl loka upatiṣṭhatetraiṣṭubham ayanaṃ bhavaty ojaskāmasyāthakāraṇidhana mājyenāmuṣmiṃl loka upatiṣṭhatejāgatam ayanaṃ bhavati paśukāmasyeḍānidhanaṃ payasāmuṣmiṃl loka upatiṣṭhatePB  añjasāryo mālyaḥ śakvarīḥ prārautsīd iti hovācālammaṃ pārijānataṃ rajanaḥkauṇayo yady enāḥ pratiṣṭhāpaṃ śakṣyatīty etad vā etāsām añjayati pratiṣṭhitā yaābhiḥ kṣipraṃ prastutya kṣipram udgāyatiPB  śakvarībhiḥ stutvā purīṣeṇa stuvatePB  paśavo vai śakvaryo gauṣṭhaḥ purīṣaṃ goṣṭham eva tat paśubhyaḥ paryasyanti tam evainān pravartyanty avisraṃsāyaPB  indro madāya vāvṛdha ity avardhanta hy etarhiPB  tāsu bārhadgiramPB  svādor itthā viṣuvata iti viṣuvān vai pañcamam ahas tāsu rāyovājīyamPB  indro yatīn sālāvṛkebhyaḥ prāyacchat teṣāṃ traya udaśiṣyanta pṛthuraśmirbṛhadgirī rāyovājas te bruvan ko na imān putrān bhariṣyatīty aham itīndro bravīttān ādhinidhāya paricāryaṃ carad vardhayaṃs tān vardhayitvābravīt kumārakā varān vṛṇīdhvam iti kṣatraṃ mahyam ity abravīt pṛthuraśmis tasmā etena pārthuraśmena kṣatraṃ prāyacchat kṣatrakāma etena stuvīta kṣatrasyaivāsya prakāśo bhavati brahmavarcasaṃ mahyam ity abravīt bṛhādgiris tasmā etena bārhadgireṇa prāyacchat brahmavarcasakāma etena stuvīta brahmavarcasī bhavatipaśūn mahyam ity abravīd rāyovājas tasmā etena rāyovājīyena paśūn prāyacchat paśukāma etena stuvīta paśumān bhavati PB  pārthuraśmaṃ rājanyāya brahmasāma kuryāt bārhadgiraṃ brāhmaṇāya rāyovājīyaṃ vaiśyāya svenaivenāṃs tad rūpeṇa samardhayati stomaḥ PB  asāvy aṃśur madāya iti gāyatrī bhavati madavad vai rasavat tṛtīyasavanaṃ madam eva tad rasaṃ dadhātiPB  abhi dyumnaṃ bṛhadyaśa ity abhīti rathantarasya rūpaṃ bṛhad iti bṛhata ubhayos saha rūpam upaity ubhau hi varṇāv etad ahaḥPB  prāṇā śiśur mahīnām iti simānāṃ rūpaṃ mahyo hi simāḥ svenaivainās tad rūpeṇa samardhayatiPB  pavasva vājasātaya iti vaiṣṇavyo nuṣṭubho bhavantiPB  yajño vai viṣṇur yad atra nāpi kriyate tad viṣṇunā yajñenāpi karotiPB  indur vājī pavate gonyoghā iti simānāṃ rūpaṃ svenaivainās tad rūpeṇa samardhayatiPB  triṣṭubhaḥ satyo jagatyo rūpeṇa tasmāj jagatīnāṃ loke kriyantePB  gāyatraṃ bhavati yad eva gāyatrasya brāhmaṇamPB  santani bhavati triṣṭupPB  akrān samudraḥ parame vidharmann iti navamasyāhnaḥ pratipad bhavatiPB  paramaṃ vā etad ahar vidharma vidharma vā etad anyair aharbhir ahar yan navamaṃ jyeṣṭhaṃ hi variṣṭhamPB  matsi vāyum
